# FEATURE_MAP.md

This file is a compatibility index and first-pass source. The maintained feature atlas now starts at [feature-map/index.md](./feature-map/index.md), with complete raw Oracle outputs under [feature-map/raw-oracle/](./feature-map/raw-oracle/) and distilled chapters under [feature-map/features/](./feature-map/features/).

Adjacent: dedicated File Search; built-in list views; ACP slash/mention portals; prompt entities; current-app commands; platform hotkey listener; config/theme preferences; escape routing; automation surfaces. Empty Recent Files | empty root with frecency rows | none | Recent Files section renders without starting Spotlight or directory scan; .appbundles/app internals suppressed | Enter root file / Cmd+K file actions / type query | Empty recents use eligibility gate; direct.app can still appear only in intentional directory browse. Plain text search | character input in main filter | type non-special text | filter_textchanges,computed_filter_textinstalled, grouped/fuzzy primary rows recomputed, selection snapshot stable | more chars / Backspace / Enter / source head / popup trigger | Selection usesSearchResult::stable_selection_key, not input-history keys. Newline rejected | pasted or programmatic newline into single-line filter | newline | filter_change.newline_ignored; canonical filter stays unchanged | previous state | Prevents multiline corruption of root query. Grouped primary results | plain or stripped query | fuzzy match | commands/scripts/scriptlets/built-ins/apps/skills/windows grouped as primary; passive rows stay below; fallback rows last | navigation / Enter / Cmd+K | mainWindowPreflight.visibleResults exposes role, action kind, type label, source name. Fallback rows | no strong primary or file/passive continuation needed | query text | fallback/continuation rows have stable selection keys and are not input-history targets | Enter visible grouped fallback | Guard: visible fallback selection executes before legacy fallback cursor. Root Files loading | eligible global filename query | type safe query | Files section appears before fallback; header says Files · Searching...; real cached/recent rows may render; continuation row remains stable | provider warms cache / query changes | Provider completion cannot mutate same-query active frame. Root Files cached frame | same query rebuilt after provider warm | query changes away/back or frame reset | cached file rows eligible at first frame build | Enter open / Cmd+K / Tab on directory | Cached rows never stream into already-visible same-query frame. Root file promotion | strong filename/stem/token match | type exact/prefix/token query | Files may promote above ordinary command/app/script/skill only when top file is strong and top primary is not strong | Enter file / query changes | Promotion disabled during loading and is grouping-only. Root directory browse | explicit path query such as ~/dev/| type path | Files section switches to bounded direct-child listing; header saysFiles · Loading folder...; no recursive search | child fragment / Tab / Shift+Tab / Enter | Directory browse intentionally may replace direct-child batch in active frame. Root directory child fragment | path plus fragment such as ~/dev/al | type/delete fragment | active directory listing reused when containing folder and hidden-file mode unchanged | refine / clear fragment / Shift+Tab | Avoids blank flash and provider restart. Files continuation row | non-empty global file query or directory browse | select continuation | Search Files for "<query>"orOpen File Search in "<folder>" | Enter opens dedicated File Search | Continuation row selection-safe, not history target. Root passive rows | enabled or explicitly selected passive sources | non-empty eligible query | Notes/Clipboard/Dictation/AI Conversations/Browser Tabs/Browser History append through passive order after Files and before fallback | Enter source action / Cmd+K actions | Metadata-only foreground rows; cache refresh must not alter same-query target. Source filter token active | standalone or attached source head | files:/f:/notes:/n:/clipboard:/c:/tabs:/t:/history:/h:/commands:/cmd:/conversations:/ai:/dictation:/d:/windows:/w: | known source head stripped; selected source enabled; primary/fallback/disallowed sources suppressed | row Enter / delete source token / add another allowed token | Source heads parse anywhere as standalone trailing-colon tokens; attached suffix searches stripped text. Uncommitted source-looking token | unsupported or quoted token | processes:/p:or quoted/unknown token | token stays literal; no source-filter mode | continue typing / delete |processes:/p: reserved until root process rows exist. Leading colon discovery | first char :| type:| menu-syntax discovery opens; not committed source syntax | choose qualifier / Escape / type partial | Source-filter-only queries do not render menu-syntax hint;; still opens capture discovery. Files source one-char query | explicit file source plus one alnum | f:s/files:s| Files search allowed even though plains root file search stays suppressed | provider/direct lookup / Enter / delete | Direct source lookup prevents first-use cache-warm-only failure. Source status chip | explicit positive source filter | source head active | non-selectable source-chip status exposed as role:"status"/kind:"sourceStatus"; possible loading/capped/empty/exhausted metadata | getElements only / no row selection | Status must not affect list count, mini sizing, scroll height, or executable rows. Source-filter input-history block | source-filter mode | Up/Down at first selectable row | Up/Down remain list navigation; launcher input-history recall disabled | leave source mode | Prevents source-filter queries from being replaced by history. Answer:

FEATURE_MAP.md Coverage Index 001 Main Menu / Script List / Menu Syntax / Actions / Shortcut Assignment 002 Dedicated File Search / Root Files / Directory Browse / File Actions 003 ACP Chat / Agent Catalog / Context Composer / Attachment Portals 001 Main Menu / Script List / Menu Syntax / Actions / Shortcut Assignment Boundaries Owns: AppView::ScriptList main launcher search; root grouped results; ScriptList filter input; main-list selection; menu-syntax trigger popup; MainList actions palette; root unified result actions; script/scriptlet/builtin/app shortcut assignment through config.ts. Adjacent: dedicated File Search; built-in list views; ACP slash/mention portals; prompt entities; current-app commands; platform hotkey listener; config/theme preferences; escape routing; automation surfaces. Empty Recent Files | empty root with frecency rows | none | Recent Files section renders without starting Spotlight or directory scan; .appbundles/app internals suppressed | Enter root file / Cmd+K file actions / type query | Empty recents use eligibility gate; direct.app can still appear only in intentional directory browse. Plain text search | character input in main filter | type non-special text | filter_textchanges,computed_filter_textinstalled, grouped/fuzzy primary rows recomputed, selection snapshot stable | more chars / Backspace / Enter / source head / popup trigger | Selection usesSearchResult::stable_selection_key, not input-history keys. Newline rejected | pasted or programmatic newline into single-line filter | newline | filter_change.newline_ignored; canonical filter stays unchanged | previous state | Prevents multiline corruption of root query. Grouped primary results | plain or stripped query | fuzzy match | commands/scripts/scriptlets/built-ins/apps/skills/windows grouped as primary; passive rows stay below; fallback rows last | navigation / Enter / Cmd+K | mainWindowPreflight.visibleResults exposes role, action kind, type label, source name. Fallback rows | no strong primary or file/passive continuation needed | query text | fallback/continuation rows have stable selection keys and are not input-history targets | Enter visible grouped fallback | Guard: visible fallback selection executes before legacy fallback cursor. Root Files loading | eligible global filename query | type safe query | Files section appears before fallback; header says Files · Searching...; real cached/recent rows may render; continuation row remains stable | provider warms cache / query changes | Provider completion cannot mutate same-query active frame. Root Files cached frame | same query rebuilt after provider warm | query changes away/back or frame reset | cached file rows eligible at first frame build | Enter open / Cmd+K / Tab on directory | Cached rows never stream into already-visible same-query frame. Root file promotion | strong filename/stem/token match | type exact/prefix/token query | Files may promote above ordinary command/app/script/skill only when top file is strong and top primary is not strong | Enter file / query changes | Promotion disabled during loading and is grouping-only. Root directory browse | explicit path query such as ~/dev/| type path | Files section switches to bounded direct-child listing; header saysFiles · Loading folder...; no recursive search | child fragment / Tab / Shift+Tab / Enter | Directory browse intentionally may replace direct-child batch in active frame. Root directory child fragment | path plus fragment such as ~/dev/al | type/delete fragment | active directory listing reused when containing folder and hidden-file mode unchanged | refine / clear fragment / Shift+Tab | Avoids blank flash and provider restart. Files continuation row | non-empty global file query or directory browse | select continuation | Search Files for "<query>"orOpen File Search in "<folder>" | Enter opens dedicated File Search | Continuation row selection-safe, not history target. Root passive rows | enabled or explicitly selected passive sources | non-empty eligible query | Notes/Clipboard/Dictation/AI Conversations/Browser Tabs/Browser History append through passive order after Files and before fallback | Enter source action / Cmd+K actions | Metadata-only foreground rows; cache refresh must not alter same-query target. Source filter token active | standalone or attached source head | files:/f:/notes:/n:/clipboard:/c:/tabs:/t:/history:/h:/commands:/cmd:/conversations:/ai:/dictation:/d:/windows:/w: | known source head stripped; selected source enabled; primary/fallback/disallowed sources suppressed | row Enter / delete source token / add another allowed token | Source heads parse anywhere as standalone trailing-colon tokens; attached suffix searches stripped text. Uncommitted source-looking token | unsupported or quoted token | processes:/p:or quoted/unknown token | token stays literal; no source-filter mode | continue typing / delete |processes:/p: reserved until root process rows exist. Leading colon discovery | first char :| type:| menu-syntax discovery opens; not committed source syntax | choose qualifier / Escape / type partial | Source-filter-only queries do not render menu-syntax hint;; still opens capture discovery. Files source-only browse | f:orfiles:with empty stripped query, usually trailing space |f: /files: | Recent Files browse even when ordinary root Files disabled; deeper browse target; 12-row source-chip page | arrows near bottom expand page / Enter / type suffix | Does not change ordinary empty-root Recent Files cap. Files source one-char query | explicit file source plus one alnum | f:s/files:s| Files search allowed even though plains root file search stays suppressed | provider/direct lookup / Enter / delete | Direct source lookup prevents first-use cache-warm-only failure. Source status chip | explicit positive source filter | source head active | non-selectable source-chip status exposed as role:"status"/kind:"sourceStatus"; possible loading/capped/empty/exhausted metadata | getElements only / no row selection | Status must not affect list count, mini sizing, scroll height, or executable rows. Source-filter input-history block | source-filter mode | Up/Down at first selectable row | Up/Down remain list navigation; launcher input-history recall disabled | leave source mode | Prevents source-filter queries from being replaced by history. Legacy trigger typed | first char ~, /, @, >, or ?| type legacy trigger | open menu-syntax popup closes if present; no popup opens from trigger state machine | special entry route or literal handling |@is legacy trigger; ACP mention picker routing is only visible throughScriptListSpecialEntry::AcpMentionPicker. Special entry route | filter matches special entry detector | e.g. file search mini, ACP slash, ACP mention, Quick Terminal, Actions Help | script_list_special_entry_routed logged; current view changes to target surface | child surface takes over | Exact trigger strings for all special entries need next pass. Home/path handoff | type ~or/...path syntax | path-like input | mini File Search opens; menu-syntax decorations cleared before first File Search paint | File Search Mini or return to ScriptList | Must not inheritf: source-chip chrome. Capture trigger popup | ;or+| type bare capture sigil |TriggerPickerSnapshotopens with CaptureTarget rows; first enabled non-footer selected | arrows / Enter / Escape / partial query |powerSyntax.captureSigilsupports;, +, or both. Partial capture trigger | capture sigil plus slug prefix | ;t/+t | popup remains open; rows filtered by target slug prefix; footer actions retained | Enter target / type whitespace/body / Escape | Footer-only result closes/no snapshot. Capture body composer | capture target plus body text | ;todo ...| open popup closes when input becomes body/composer state | normal main-list search/capture mode | Exact terminal grammar is clipped; verify with fullmenu_syntax module. Advanced query popup | leading :|:/:source/:has| qualifier rows shown; partial query highlights title/meta; footer actions clickable | InsertToken / OpenHelp / Escape | Leading: is discovery, not source syntax. Terminal qualifier token | typed/selected qualifier value | has:shortcut| terminal token participates in menu syntax/search; popup token can be asserted in promptPopupgetElements| Enter result / Backspace to partial | Full parser semantics forhas:shortcut need next pass. Trigger picker footer action | popup contains FooterAction | mouse click or explicit selection only | row maps to InlinePickerRowKind::Action; no default keyboard selection; no partial highlights | OpenHelp / OpenCaptures / CreateHandler / AiScaffoldHandler | Enabled footer rows clickable but skipped by default selection. Trigger picker disabled rows | popup snapshot has disabled rows | arrows/selection preserve | disabled rows not default-selected; if previous row disabled, selection moves to first enabled | select enabled / close | preserve_or_pick_first_enabled owns this. Trigger popup ReplaceInput keep-open | picker outcome ReplaceInput keep_open | Enter accepted row | filter, pending sync, computed text updated; grouped cache invalidated; state machine reruns | popup update/open | Used for multi-step token insertion. Trigger popup ReplaceInput close | picker outcome ReplaceInput keep_open false | Enter accepted row | popup state cleared; window closed; suppressed filter set to accepted text | input changes clears suppression | Prevents immediate reopen on same accepted text. Exhaustiveness Notes Include every explicit scenario/state you can infer from the bundle. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: full src/scripts/search/unified.rs, src/scripts/search/prefix_filters.rs, and crate::menu_syntax source bodies were listed in the directory map but not included as source snippets; exact parser rows, qualifier value semantics, and grouped ranking implementation need a focused pass. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: full src/render_script_list/mod.rs key handler after line 969 is clipped; exact Cmd+Enter, normal non-file Tab, action shortcut execution, and popup-first routing order need source expansion. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: src/main_entry/runtime_stdin_match_simulate_key.rs is listed but not included; physical/stdin parity is only evidenced through verification text for Enter action activation. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Remove Shortcut runtime implementation in src/app_actions/handle_action/shortcuts.rs is not in the bundle; config write contract is clear, but live hotkey unregister/refresh/HUD behavior needs another pass. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: preview/info panel affordances are only visible through shortcut display audits, not renderer snippets; main-list right-side preview/detail/shortcut glyph visual states need app_render/preview_panel.rs and focused_info.rs. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: exact action IDs/labels for script context actions such as Add Shortcut, Update Shortcut, Remove Shortcut, Add/Edit Alias, and Copy Deep Link need src/actions/builders/script_context.rs full body and shortcut action handlers. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: agent/agent-chat shortcut rows are inferred only through built-in/command identity rules; dedicated Agent Catalog or agent row shortcut assignment needs the next feature slice or broader source bundle. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: menu-syntax popup mouse handling is partially visible; row click, mouse arm/disarm, and footer click edge cases need full menu_syntax_trigger_popup_window.rs. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: empty/default main menu exact row order, suggested defaults renderer, info/preview affordances, and visual styling need full render/grouping sources plus a state-first getElements capture.

002 Dedicated File Search / Root Files / Directory Browse / File Actions Boundaries Owns: dedicated File Search surface; ~ / ~/... mini handoff; full file-search preview browser; root Files / Recent Files passive source; root directory browse; files: / f: source-filtered Files mode; file row actions; file attach flows; native drag-out rows. Includes the visible thresholds: ordinary root min 3 chars; two-character alphanumeric with digit allowed; explicit f:/files: one/two ASCII alphanumeric allowed; advanced kMDItem and directory paths excluded from global root search. Includes the visible limits: root result cache limit 24; root browse source limit 96; root browse render limit 12; source-chip initial/page visible rows 12; recent hydrate deeper than empty render cap; dedicated loading skeleton 6 rows. Includes the visible failure modes: late provider active-frame mutation, status-as-row regression, .app leakage in global root Files/recents, stale hidden-mode cache, Quick Look missing path/blocking spawn, native drag stale hover/focus, file action target reuse, unknown root action fallthrough, actions popup semantic-surface clobber. 004 MCP Resources / SDK / Protocol Automation Boundaries Owns: stdin JSONL ingress, protocol envelope/deprecation observation, ExternalCommand, fire-and-forget stdin control, protocol query/automation messages, transaction waitFor/batch, automation target identity, MCP resources, MCP tools, SDK automation helpers, SDK reference resource, agentic proof routing. Adjacent: prompt rendering, ACP chat/setup internals, notes/editor internals, filterable built-in surfaces, native screenshot capture, script execution runtime, OS/AppKit bridges, tray/menu/window registries. Source anchors: src/protocol/{version.rs,deprecations.rs,ingress.rs,message/variants/query_ops.rs,types/{automation_window.rs,batch_wait.rs},transaction_executor.rs}, src/stdin_commands/mod.rs, src/main_entry/runtime_stdin*.rs, src/mcp_resources/{mod.rs,transaction_resources.rs}, src/mcp_protocol/mod.rs, src/mcp_server/mod.rs, src/mcp_script_tools.rs, src/mcp_kit_tools.rs, src/mcp_computer_use_tools.rs, scripts/kit-sdk.ts, scripts/agentic/index.ts mcp-sdk-protocol-map Verification anchors: tests/protocol_{batch,wait_for,wait_for_contract,ingress_golden}.rs, tests/mcp_resource_drift.rs, tests/mcp_resources_sdk_reference.rs, tests/mcp_protocol_golden.rs, tests/sdk_automation_{runtime,contracts}.rs, tests/source_audits/{trigger_builtin_registry_consistency,trigger_builtin_sdk_literals,sdk_computer_use_contract}.rs. Protocol State Map Version envelope | read_wire_version / observe_ingress | JSON object with optional protocolVersion:number | absent = legacy v1; accepted range from MIN_PROTOCOL_VERSION..=CURRENT_PROTOCOL_VERSION; outbound attach_current_version stamps current | ingress observation / response envelopes | non-object, non-integer, negative, overflow, too-old, too-new are typed errors. Stdin version gate | parse_stdin_command | raw stdin JSONL object | strips protocolVersion before command parse; bundle tests show absent/v1 accepted and explicit v2 rejected by stdin gate | stdin_command_parsed or stdin_parse_failed | split contract visible: protocol envelope current is v2, stdin gate test still expects v1; NEEDS_NEXT_PASS if changing. Deprecation registry | validate_deprecations / DEPRECATED_FIELDS | kind, body, ProtocolVersion | triggerBuiltin.name warns from v2, replacement builtinId, removed at v3 | ProtocolDeprecationWarning / ProtocolDeprecationError::FieldRemoved | parser can call with legacy default and still warn correctly. Ingress observation | observe_ingress / observe_value | raw JSONL line or parsed Value | returns ObservedIngress { kind, version, warnings, deprecation_error } | protocol-stats counter for unsupported versions | bad JSON/non-object/unsupported envelope are IngressObserveError; unsupported-version observer is health telemetry, not a full parser replacement. Unsupported protocol telemetry | record_unsupported_version | raw line with out-of-range protocolVersion | bumps stdin_unsupported_protocol_version_total; rate-limited warn | kit://diagnostics/protocol-stats health flag | valid v2, legacy no-envelope, malformed JSON, non-object root, non-integer version do not bump. Command parser | parse_stdin_command | ExternalCommand first, SDK Message fallback second | known automation verb with wrong payload returns automation_payload_mismatch; unknown verb falls through to SDK message parser | parse receipt / session.sh rpc parse_error fallback | ExternalCommand has deny_unknown_fields; field typos are not silent. Request correlation | ExternalCommandRequestId / protocol requestId | transparent String, optional on many externals, required on protocol queries | response-capable commands echo verbatim; no cap/truncation except 16 KiB stdin line cap | response envelope, logs, lenient parse-error cid | long IDs round-trip; charset-unsafe IDs use unscoped parse-error fallback. show | stdin {"type":"show","requestId"?} | no payload besides optional requestId | shows main window, marks shown, syncs main automation window, focuses main filter | parse receipt only; follow with getState / getElements / listAutomationWindows | fire-and-forget; no showResult. hide | stdin {"type":"hide","requestId"?} | no payload besides optional requestId | reset to ScriptList, rekey semanticSurface=scriptList, defer hide | parse receipt only; follow with getState / listAutomationWindows | reset-before-rekey order is contract; no hideResult. setFilter | stdin {"type":"setFilter","text":string,"requestId"?} | text up to stdin line cap | writes main filter text and notifies | follow with getState.inputValue, visibleChoiceCount, getElements | no visible response envelope in dispatcher snippets; inputValue echoes verbatim. triggerBuiltin | stdin {"type":"triggerBuiltin","builtinId":string,"requestId"?} or deprecated name | exactly one of builtinId or name | dispatches built-in and rekeys main automation surface from current view | follow with getState.surfaceContract, getElements, automation window registry | both/neither rejected; canonical IDs are drift-audited; legacy literals source-audited. simulateKey | stdin {"type":"simulateKey","key":string,"modifiers"?:KeyModifier[],"requestId"?} | modifiers include cmd, shift, option, control; aliases include meta for cmd | routes per-view key handling; Cmd+K toggles actions where host exists; Escape routes popup-first/filter/go-back/hide | parse receipt only; follow with getState / getElements / inspectAutomationWindow | fire-and-forget; unknown modifier rejected; no simulateKeyResult. run | stdin {"type":"run","path":string,"requestId"?} | script path | PromptMessage::RunScript into prompt runtime | logs/requestId; follow script/prompt state | script execution behavior is adjacent. openNotes | stdin {"type":"openNotes"} | no requestId visible in variant | opens Notes window | listAutomationWindows, inspectAutomationWindow, getElements(target) | Notes-targeted batch.setInput routes by Notes mode. openAbout | stdin {"type":"openAbout"} | no requestId visible in variant | opens in-window About surface without tray menu | getState / getElements About chrome | automation-only route listed in stdin commands resource. AI/ACP open aliases | openAi, openMiniAi, openAiWithMockData, openMiniAiWithMockData, showAiCommandBar | no args in visible tests | open Agent Chat / command bar compatibility routes | getAcpState, waitFor acpReady, getElements(target) | ACP feature details remain adjacent. AI/ACP input | setAiSearch, setAiInput, setAcpInput, pasteClipboardIntoAcp, pushDictationResult | text/search/submit/target/transcript/requestId shapes | drives AI/ACP search, composer, clipboard paste, dictation injection | getAcpState, getAcpTestProbe, waitFor ACP conditions | setAcpInput "/" is proof path for prompt popup. AI state | getAiWindowState | optional requestId | returns AI window state if visible path succeeds | response envelope/logs | older AI-window-specific probe; adjacent to ACP state. Debug grid | showGrid / hideGrid | gridSize, showBounds, showBoxModel, showAlignmentGuides, showDimensions, depth=all or components | toggles debug overlay | screenshot/layout proof | visual/debug-only protocol state. Capture by title | captureWindow | { title, path, requestId? } | captures window with title pattern to file | file/visual audit | distinct from protocol captureScreenshot and MCP computer/capture_native_window. Fallback/action routes | executeFallback, triggerAction, showShortcutRecorder | fallbackId/input, actionId/host, commandId/commandName | invokes fallback/action/shortcut-recorder routes | follow with state/elements/logs | action host behavior adjacent to Actions feature. Config fingerprint | getConfigFingerprint | optional requestId | emits current config receipt {path,len,modified_ms,ok,error_code?} | config_fingerprint_result / response-capable receipt | read-only disk proof; config_file_missing distinguished. Protocol getState | stdin protocol {"type":"getState","requestId":string,"target"?} | target optional | stateResult main-window contract | response envelope | non-main explicit targets return diagnostic promptType:"unsupported" or target_resolution_failed. stateResult receipts | collect_state | active main app state | promptType, promptId, inputValue, counts, selected/focused, windowVisible, screenshotIdentity, surfaceContract, popup/footer/decorations where present | state-first proof | choiceCount dataset and visibleChoiceCount filter-aware; invariant visibleChoiceCount <= choiceCount. getElements | stdin protocol {"type":"getElements","requestId":string,"limit"?, "target"?} | optional limit/target | elementsResult visible elements, totalCount, truncated, focused/selected semantic IDs, warnings | response envelope | rows may include role/kind/source/status/selectable/actionDisabled/footer buttons. getLayoutInfo | stdin protocol visible in command map | requestId; full payload elided | layout info receipt | response envelope | NEEDS_NEXT_PASS for exact input/result schema. captureScreenshot | query surface listed in lat | target/path/options not fully visible | screenshot capture receipt | response envelope/file proof | NEEDS_NEXT_PASS for exact protocol shape; distinct from captureWindow and computer capture. getAcpState | stdin protocol command map | requestId + optional target | ACP state snapshot or absent state | response envelope | target-specific ACP state preferred over targeted getState. getAcpTestProbe | scope mentions if visible | not expanded in snippets | probe receipt | response envelope | NEEDS_NEXT_PASS for exact visibility, payload, and result schema. performAcpSetupAction | stdin protocol command map | requestId + setup action payload elided | mutates ACP setup flow | response envelope | ACP setup specifics adjacent. inspectAutomationWindow | stdin protocol command map | requestId + AutomationWindowTarget | automation window/surface inspection | response envelope | preferred for non-main target identity and diagnostics. listAutomationWindows | stdin protocol command map | requestId | automation window registry snapshot | response envelope | pairs with focusedAutomationWindowId; supports exact target promotion. simulateGpuiEvent | stdin protocol command map | requestId + target/event payload elided | GPUI-side event dispatch without OS focus | response envelope | used for detached ACP proof; native input remains last resort. waitFor | stdin protocol {"type":"waitFor","requestId",condition,timeout?,pollInterval?,trace?,target?} | named or detailed condition | waitForResult {success,elapsed,error?,trace?} | transaction trace/resource | timeout/poll defaults; invalid condition returns structured error. batch | stdin protocol {"type":"batch","requestId",commands,options?,trace?,target?} | command array + BatchOptions | batchResult {success,results,failedAt?,totalElapsed,trace?} | transaction trace/resource | request ids replay only for identical stable fingerprint. Batch primitive setInput | BatchCommand::SetInput | {type:"setInput",text} | writes target input | result entry + after snapshot | Notes target dispatches to Notes editor or embedded ACP composer by mode. Batch primitive waitFor | BatchCommand::WaitFor | condition + timeout/pollInterval | polls UiStateSnapshot | result entry with elapsed/error | ACP waits read ACP fields/probe; setup-card waits rejected until populated. Batch selection primitives | selectByValue, selectBySemanticId | value/semanticId + submit | selects visible choice/element, optionally submits | result entry | failure suggests getElements / waitFor elementExists. Batch compound commands | forceSubmit, filterAndSelect, typeAndSubmit | parsed by protocol | executor marks unsupported where not wired | structured unsupported error/suggestion | caller should compose primitives. Transaction replay | execute_wait_for / execute_batch | reused requestId | same fingerprint returns prior trace/result; different payload rejects | trace log/resource | stable idempotency contract. Session send receipt | session.sh send --await-parse | JSON + optional timeout | returns {status:"ok",sent:true} by default; await returns parsed, parseError, or timeout | log-offset/parse-event correlation | non-numeric timeout = invalid_timeout; flag-before-json = flag_as_command. Session rpc parse recovery | session.sh rpc --expect TYPE | typed response wait | parse failure short-circuits/fallbacks to {status:"error",error:{code:"parse_error"}} | app.log cid scan / await-response preempt scan | distinguishes parse error from generic timeout. Automation Query Matrix getState | main target, omitted target, Main, Focused, or explicit main | stateResult main-window state | non-main target => promptType:"unsupported"; target resolve failure => target_resolution_failed | runtime proof uses response envelope keyed by requestId. getState.choiceCount/visibleChoiceCount | filterable main surfaces | dataset count + filter-aware visible count | invariant break if visibleChoiceCount > choiceCount or filtering mutates dataset count | pinned by state count contract tests. getState.surfaceContract | resolved main window | surfaceKind, vocabulary, focus/keyboard/actions/proof/visual policy, automationSemanticSurface, nativeFooterSurface | omitted on secondary target diagnostics | proof surface for migrated launcher surfaces. getState.activePopupContract | actions popup/dialog active | attached popup contract with SurfaceKind::ActionsDialog | absent when no attached popup | proves overlay policy without pixel inspection. getState.activeFooter | native footer installed or fallback visible | expected/requested/active native footer ids, AppKit host, GPUI fallback, buttons, disabled reasons, mismatch marker | stale native footer marked mismatch | getElements also emits footer row/button elements. getState.filterInputDecorations | ScriptList live decoration receipt | rendered input text + chip ranges/roles | omitted Protocol State Map Version envelope | read_wire_version / observe_ingress | JSON object with optional protocolVersion:number | absent = legacy v1; accepted range from MIN_PROTOCOL_VERSION..=CURRENT_PROTOCOL_VERSION; outbound attach_current_version stamps current | ingress observation / response envelopes | non-object, non-integer, negative, overflow, too-old, too-new are typed errors. Stdin version gate | parse_stdin_command | raw stdin JSONL object | strips protocolVersion before command parse; bundle tests show absent/v1 accepted and explicit v2 rejected by stdin gate | stdin_command_parsed or stdin_parse_failed | split contract visible: protocol envelope current is v2, stdin gate test still expects v1; NEEDS_NEXT_PASS if changing. Deprecation registry | validate_deprecations / DEPRECATED_FIELDS | kind, body, ProtocolVersion | triggerBuiltin.name warns from v2, replacement builtinId, removed at v3 | ProtocolDeprecationWarning / ProtocolDeprecationError::FieldRemoved | parser can call with legacy default and still warn correctly. Ingress observation | observe_ingress / observe_value | raw JSONL line or parsed Value | returns ObservedIngress { kind, version, warnings, deprecation_error } | protocol-stats counter for unsupported versions | bad JSON/non-object/unsupported envelope are IngressObserveError; unsupported-version observer is health telemetry, not a full parser replacement. Unsupported protocol telemetry | record_unsupported_version | raw line with out-of-range protocolVersion | bumps stdin_unsupported_protocol_version_total; rate-limited warn | kit://diagnostics/protocol-stats health flag | valid v2, legacy no-envelope, malformed JSON, non-object root, non-integer version do not bump. Command parser | parse_stdin_command | ExternalCommand first, SDK Message fallback second | known automation verb with wrong payload returns automation_payload_mismatch; unknown verb falls through to SDK message parser | parse receipt / session.sh rpc parse_error fallback | ExternalCommand has deny_unknown_fields; field typos are not silent. Request correlation | ExternalCommandRequestId / protocol requestId | transparent String, optional on many externals, required on protocol queries | response-capable commands echo verbatim; no cap/truncation except 16 KiB stdin line cap | response envelope, logs, lenient parse-error cid | long IDs round-trip; charset-unsafe IDs use unscoped parse-error fallback. show | stdin {"type":"show","requestId"?} | no payload besides optional requestId | shows main window, marks shown, syncs main automation window, focuses main filter | parse receipt only; follow with getState / getElements / listAutomationWindows | fire-and-forget; no showResult. hide | stdin {"type":"hide","requestId"?} | no payload besides optional requestId | reset to ScriptList, rekey semanticSurface=scriptList, defer hide | parse receipt only; follow with getState / listAutomationWindows | reset-before-rekey order is contract; no hideResult. setFilter | stdin {"type":"setFilter","text":string,"requestId"?} | text up to stdin line cap | writes main filter text and notifies | follow with getState.inputValue, visibleChoiceCount, getElements | no visible response envelope in dispatcher snippets; inputValue echoes verbatim. triggerBuiltin | stdin {"type":"triggerBuiltin","builtinId":string,"requestId"?} or deprecated name | exactly one of builtinId or name | dispatches built-in and rekeys main automation surface from current view | follow with getState.surfaceContract, getElements, automation window registry | both/neither rejected; canonical IDs are drift-audited; legacy literals source-audited. simulateKey | stdin {"type":"simulateKey","key":string,"modifiers"?:KeyModifier[],"requestId"?} | modifiers include cmd, shift, option, control; aliases include meta for cmd | routes per-view key handling; Cmd+K toggles actions where host exists; Escape routes popup-first/filter/go-back/hide | parse receipt only; follow with getState / getElements / inspectAutomationWindow | fire-and-forget; unknown modifier rejected; no simulateKeyResult. run | stdin {"type":"run","path":string,"requestId"?} | script path | PromptMessage::RunScript into prompt runtime | logs/requestId; follow script/prompt state | script execution behavior is adjacent. openNotes | stdin {"type":"openNotes"} | no requestId visible in variant | opens Notes window | listAutomationWindows, inspectAutomationWindow, getElements(target) | Notes-targeted batch.setInput routes by Notes mode. openAbout | stdin {"type":"openAbout"} | no requestId visible in variant | opens in-window About surface without tray menu | getState / getElements About chrome | automation-only route listed in stdin commands resource. Protocol getState | stdin protocol {"type":"getState","requestId":string,"target"?} | target optional | stateResult main-window contract | response envelope | non-main explicit targets return diagnostic promptType:"unsupported" or target_resolution_failed. stateResult receipts | collect_state | active main app state | promptType, promptId, inputValue, counts, selected/focused, windowVisible, screenshotIdentity, surfaceContract, popup/footer/decorations where present | state-first proof | choiceCount dataset and visibleChoiceCount filter-aware; invariant visibleChoiceCount <= choiceCount. getElements | stdin protocol {"type":"getElements","requestId":string,"limit"?, "target"?} | optional limit/target | elementsResult visible elements, totalCount, truncated, focused/selected semantic IDs, warnings | response envelope | rows may include role/kind/source/status/selectable/actionDisabled/footer buttons. getLayoutInfo | stdin protocol visible in command map | requestId; full payload elided | layout info receipt | response envelope | NEEDS_NEXT_PASS for exact input/result schema. captureScreenshot | query surface listed in lat | target/path/options not fully visible | screenshot capture receipt | response envelope/file proof | NEEDS_NEXT_PASS for exact protocol shape; distinct from captureWindow and computer capture. getAcpState | stdin protocol command map | requestId + optional target | ACP state snapshot or absent state | response envelope | target-specific ACP state preferred over targeted getState. getAcpTestProbe | scope mentions if visible | not expanded in snippets | probe receipt | response envelope | NEEDS_NEXT_PASS for exact visibility, payload, and result schema. performAcpSetupAction | stdin protocol command map | requestId + setup action payload elided | mutates ACP setup flow | response envelope | ACP setup specifics adjacent. inspectAutomationWindow | stdin protocol command map | requestId + AutomationWindowTarget | automation window/surface inspection | response envelope | preferred for non-main target identity and diagnostics. listAutomationWindows | stdin protocol command map | requestId | automation window registry snapshot | response envelope | pairs with focusedAutomationWindowId; invalid condition returns structured error. batch | stdin protocol {"type":"batch","requestId",commands,options?,trace?,target?} | command array + BatchOptions | batchResult {success,results,failedAt?,totalElapsed,trace?} | transaction trace/resource | request ids replay only for identical stable fingerprint. Exhaustiveness Notes Included every visible surface in the requested slice: Clipboard History, App Launcher, Window Switcher, Browser Tabs, Emoji Picker, Process Manager, plus shared trigger/filter/navigation/actions/protocol contracts. Included dedicated-view and root-passive distinctions for Clipboard History and Browser Tabs; these must not be collapsed because root sources are metadata-only, opt-in, capped, and passive while dedicated views own direct activation/filterable UI. Included hidden/security/exclusion states visible in bundle: hiddenCommands launcher materialization filter with programmatic resolution; root clipboard metadata-only/no raw content; root browser tabs metadata-only/no page content/favicons/cookies/downloads/network; clipboard exclusion hook should_exclude_clipboard; config gates for built-ins/passive sources. Included count asymmetries: Clipboard choiceCount=dataset, visibleChoiceCount=filter; Emoji choiceCount=all EMOJIS, visibleChoiceCount=search/category result; matrix requires visible count never exceed choice count. Included visual proof states: surfaceContract, automationSemanticSurface, list semantic ids, attached activePopupContract, PromptChromeAudit layout modes, mini/full sizing, matrix proof invariants, fallback collector failure modes. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Full src/app_impl/trigger_builtin_dispatch.rs, src/app_impl/routes.rs, src/main_sections/app_view_state.rs, src/app_layout/collect_elements.rs, and src/prompt_handler/mod.rs bodies were not fully present in the bundle; route/state/elements details above rely on lat/test/source-audit anchors rather than complete source bodies. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Clipboard Actions Dialog full catalog/action ids/shortcuts for Open With, Reveal in Finder, Copy, Share, Delete, Clear, Attach, Pin/Unpin should be mapped from the action owner/handle_action bodies. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Emoji Picker Actions Dialog catalog/action ids/shortcuts beyond paste behavior should be mapped from ActionsDialogHost::EmojiPicker action owner. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Process Manager exact row actions, Enter semantics, Stop All placement/shortcut, copy-details action, cleanup action, and user-facing confirmation/error states need full process_manager renderer/action handler context. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: App Launcher scan/cache/icon details need full src/app_launcher/scanning.rs, launch.rs, core_types.rs, and renderer row body; current bundle proves recursive vendor-folder .app leaf scanning and no dedicated Cmd+K actions but not every icon/cache fallback. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Window Switcher action catalog for tile/manage/focus and permission/error UI needs full window_control and action host context. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Browser Tabs provider-specific errors, ranking score fields, provider labels/icons, and activation failure toasts need full browser_tabs module and dispatch preload body. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Paste Sequentially visible states and receipts need full clipboard_history/paste_sequential and built-in execution path; bundle proves registry/catalog/export surface but not every sequence transition.
