Shared Actions Dialog | Navigate actions | ArrowUp/ArrowDown | skips SectionHeader; clamps to selectable GroupedActionItem::Item | selectedActionId never header | actions dialog selection/arrow tests. Shared Actions Dialog | Execute/drill-down | Enter | Drill-down route lookup before terminal on_select; terminal action may close or keep host | Executed or DrillDownPushed | actions dialog enter routing contract. Visual/Protocol Matrix Shared | surfaceContract per AppView::surface_contract()/SurfaceKind | getState.stateResult.surfaceContract.surfaceKind; automationSemanticSurface; semanticSurface registry re-key after triggerBuiltin | Missing AppView arm leaves semantic surface stale or fallback collector warning | lat.md/surfaces; lat.md/automation#Window metadata. Shared | Mini vs Full sizing | Mini default: emoji, app launcher, window switcher, browser tabs, process manager; Full: clipboard history due preview pane | Deferred resize must not re-widen Mini or narrow preview Full | builtins sizing note/tests. Shared | Focused input/list chrome | getElements includes named filter input + list semantic id; focusedSemanticId stable | Missing collect arm falls to panel:current-view and collector_used_current_view_fallback | browser tabs collect arm contract; matrix. Shared | Matrix proof | Empty and filtered receipts sampled via real triggerBuiltin; filter reset per case | visibleChoiceCount > choiceCount, list count mismatch, or insufficient totalCount fails | filterable_surface_agentic_matrix_contract. Shared | Attached actions popup | Active popup attached to parent main automation id, preserves parent semanticSurface | Upsert hardcodes scriptList; Cmd+K dropped by missing per-view arm | lat.md/automation#Window metadata; actions popup parent tests. Clipboard History | Expanded scaffold + preview pane | PromptChromeAudit::expanded("clipboard_history"); render_expanded_view_scaffold_with_hints; header count "{} entries" | Using PromptFooter/custom hardcoded footer or losing wheel intercept fails source audit | clipboard chrome audit. Clipboard History | Row ids/roles | collect_named_rows("clipboard-filter","clipboard-history", rows); rows from cached_clipboard_entries narrowed by variant filter | getElements emits full dataset when filter active | clipboard getElements contract. Clipboard History | Counts | choiceCount=entries.len; visibleChoiceCount=filtered_count; filter case-insensitive against text_preview | Filter miss indistinguishable from empty dataset if slots swapped | clipboard state receipt contract. Clipboard History | Preview partial state | Preview panel labels content type/time; fallback notice when full payload unavailable | Claims full content when only cached preview present | clipboard preview source. Clipboard History root | Metadata-only passive rows | Root grouping uses bounded metadata, eligible content types only, no get_entry_content | Privacy leak by reading raw clipboard content during grouping | root clipboard audit. App Launcher | Minimal list mini chrome | PromptChromeAudit::minimal_list; footer only "↵ Launch" + "Esc Back"; no ⌘K Actions | Dead action hint or route advertised | app launcher source audits. App Launcher | Visible rows | getElements uses app_launcher_visible_row_names(filter); getState uses app_launcher_dataset_and_visible_counts(filter) | Raw dataset indexing/filter drift | app launcher visible rows test. Window Switcher | Mini list rows | Rows filtered by displayed app — title string | Filtering hidden fields creates protocol/visual mismatch | filterable subview contract. Window Switcher | Trigger receipt | triggerBuiltin windows routes to FilterableView::WindowSwitcher, caches list_windows, sets AppView::WindowSwitcherView, resize:true | Missing alias/planner/dispatcher arm | window switcher trigger contract. Browser Tabs | Compact single-column shell | Shared input, header padding, SectionDivider, render_simple_hint_strip, key context "browser_tabs" | Fake custom cursor or missing shared input/footer | browser tabs source audit. Browser Tabs | Filter-aware elements | getElements arm calls fuzzy_search_browser_tabs; row string display_title(); semantic ids "browser-tabs-filter"/"browser-tabs" | Raw .contains drift from renderer fuzzy ranking | browser tabs collect contract. Browser Tabs root | Passive snapshot cache | Root source reads cached tab metadata; background refresh warms future frames only | Late provider work shifts same-query selected target/visible rows | root passive frame stability notes. Emoji Picker | Grid chrome | PromptChromeAudit::grid; shared three-key footer via universal_prompt_hints; no custom "↵ Copy"/"Esc Back" | Footer lies about paste behavior or custom stale labels | emoji source audits. Emoji Picker | Count asymmetry | choiceCount from EMOJIS; visibleChoiceCount from search_emojis(filter); tuple order dataset then visible | visibleChoiceCount equals full dataset or slots swapped | emoji state count test. Emoji Picker | Grid/list elements | Uniform list; emoji_scroll_handle; scrollbar overlay; row height from GRID_ROW_HEIGHT | Scrollbar/list drift or wrong row height | emoji source audits. Emoji Picker | Arrow proof | Up/Down intercepted before input catchall; stops propagation | Input consumes arrows and moves text cursor instead of selected emoji | emoji arrow contract. Process Manager | Visible row owner | process_manager_visible_row_names; process_manager_dataset_and_visible_counts; process_manager_visible_target_rows | Raw cached_processes.get(selected_index) drift | process visible rows tests. Process Manager | Refresh state | 2s poll only while ProcessManagerView; post-refresh/post-stop clamp to visible rows | Selection points past list or raw cache after stop | process renderer/source. Process Manager | Visual empty/destructive click | Empty states centered; row/Stop All click stops propagation; secondary text uses AppChromeColors | Parent surface double-handles destructive click or raw theme text | process visible rows contract. Process Manager | Trigger receipt | triggerBuiltin processes routes to FilterableView::ProcessManager; seeds sorted active processes; pending focus main filter; deferred resize | Missing alias/planner/dispatcher seed | trigger process manager contract. Exhaustiveness Notes Included every visible surface in the requested slice: Clipboard History, App Launcher, Window Switcher, Browser Tabs, Emoji Picker, Process Manager, plus shared trigger/filter/navigation/actions/protocol contracts. Included dedicated-view and root-passive distinctions for Clipboard History and Browser Tabs; these must not be collapsed because root sources are metadata-only, opt-in, capped, and passive while dedicated views own direct activation/filterable UI. Included hidden/security/exclusion states visible in bundle: hiddenCommands launcher materialization filter with programmatic resolution; root clipboard metadata-only/no raw content; root browser tabs metadata-only/no page content/favicons/cookies/downloads/network; clipboard exclusion hook should_exclude_clipboard; config gates for built-ins/passive sources. Included count asymmetries: Clipboard choiceCount=dataset, visibleChoiceCount=filter; Emoji choiceCount=all EMOJIS, visibleChoiceCount=search/category result; matrix requires visible count never exceed choice count. Included visual proof states: surfaceContract, automationSemanticSurface, list semantic ids, attached activePopupContract, PromptChromeAudit layout modes, mini/full sizing, matrix proof invariants, fallback collector failure modes. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Full src/app_impl/trigger_builtin_dispatch.rs, src/app_impl/routes.rs, src/main_sections/app_view_state.rs, src/app_layout/collect_elements.rs, and src/prompt_handler/mod.rs bodies were not fully present in the bundle; route/state/elements details above rely on lat/test/source-audit anchors rather than complete source bodies. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Clipboard Actions Dialog full catalog/action ids/shortcuts for Open With, Reveal in Finder, Copy, Share, Delete, Clear, Attach, Pin/Unpin should be mapped from the action owner/handle_action bodies. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Emoji Picker Actions Dialog catalog/action ids/shortcuts beyond paste behavior should be mapped from ActionsDialogHost::EmojiPicker action owner. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Process Manager exact row actions, Enter semantics, Stop All placement/shortcut, copy-details action, cleanup action, and user-facing confirmation/error states need full process_manager renderer/action handler context. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: App Launcher scan/cache/icon details need full src/app_launcher/scanning.rs, launch.rs, core_types.rs, and renderer row body; current bundle proves recursive vendor-folder .app leaf scanning and no dedicated Cmd+K actions but not every icon/cache fallback. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Window Switcher action catalog for tile/manage/focus and permission/error UI needs full window_control and action host context. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Browser Tabs provider-specific errors, ranking score fields, provider labels/icons, and activation failure toasts need full browser_tabs module and dispatch preload body. NEEDS_NEXT_PASS: Paste Sequentially visible states and receipts need full clipboard_history/paste_sequential and built-in execution path; bundle proves registry/catalog/export surface but not every sequence transition. Suggested next feature: 006 Notes Window / Notes Browse / Notes-hosted ACP


<!-- Source: Oracle session notes-window-feature-map, captured 2026-05-15. -->


006 Notes Window / Notes Browse / Notes-hosted ACP Boundaries Owns: Dedicated floating NotesApp host: editor state, note list/trash modes, Notes window bounds, hover/focus/chrome, local actions UI, local note switcher, Markdown editor/preview, autosave, auto-resize, clipboard/export/deeplink/quicklink, soft-delete/restore/permanent-delete flows. Notes-hosted ACP: opening/reusing embedded AcpChatView, Notes-owned ACP callbacks, Notes ACP footer host, Notes ACP actions popup, Notes ACP history popup, Notes-specific ACP close/focus behavior, note-cart handoff, note-target staging, stale-hosted-context cleanup, draft snapshot restore across agent switch. Notes Browse expanded attachment portal surface in src/render_builtins/notes_browse.rs: searchable active-note list, preview pane, note attach target construction, selection/scroll synchronization, portal cancel/attach semantics. Notes automation identity: AutomationWindowKind::Notes, stable id="notes" parent for actions, semanticSurface:"notes", targeted getState/getElements/waitFor/batch behavior. lat.md/notes.md and lat.md/tests/notes-acp.md contracts for Notes behavior, architecture, and tests. Does not own: Main launcher ACP cache, main-panel ACP surface placement, detached ACP popup lifecycle, generic AcpChatView composer internals except where Notes host callbacks/staging require host-specific contracts. Generic attachment portal machinery, File/Clipboard/Browser/Dictation portals, generic actions-popup implementation, generic command-bar/action registry behavior outside the Notes parent/focus contract. Root unified Notes search ranking/opening except the boundary that root note rows must use open_note_in_notes_window, not the toggle-open helper. Quick Terminal / PTY harness flows. Adjacent feature dependencies: $acp-chat-core: ACP lifecycle, footer, actions, model/agent/session behavior. $acp-context-composer: inline context chips, @history, pending portal sessions, pasted/mention token state. $actions-popups: shared ACP actions dialog chrome, parented actions windows, close/focus behavior. $protocol-automation: Notes-targeted getState, getElements, waitFor, batch, automation registry identity. $agentic-testing: state-first runtime receipts and cleanup. $platform-windowing-macos: floating panel, setCanHide:false, AppKit focus/hide independence. $lat-md: lat.md updates plus lat check whenever behavior/contracts/tests change. Notes is explicitly documented as a separate floating host with its own editor state, actions UI, list/trash modes, and reusable embedded ACP surface. notes-window-feature-map User Stories As a user, I can open Notes as a separate floating window that does not behave like a launcher panel clone. As a user, I can create a new note, create a note from clipboard, type Markdown, preview Markdown, use formatting helpers, and rely on debounced save. As a user, I can browse/switch notes, search within the current note, search across notes, pin notes, jump through note history, and sort notes. As a user, I can delete notes into Trash, view Trash, restore notes, permanently delete notes, and empty Trash. As a user, I can copy a note as Markdown, copy a deeplink, create a Markdown quicklink, and copy/export HTML-style output. As a user, I can send the current note/selection/cart to Agent Chat inside the Notes window without opening the main launcher ACP. As a user, I can switch between Notes editor mode and Notes-hosted ACP mode while keeping the embedded ACP conversation/draft when reuse is intended. As a user, I can open Notes-hosted ACP actions, change agent/model/history, and have actions apply to the originating embedded ACP view rather than a replaced/stale view. As a user, I can open local ACP History from Notes-hosted ACP and attach/cancel through the same staged replacement contract used elsewhere. As a user, I can use Notes Browse as an attachment portal to search active notes, preview content, attach a selected note, or cancel cleanly. As an automation user, I can target Notes as {kind:"notes"} and not accidentally hit the main window. The targeting test registers main and Notes separately, resolves Notes by kind/title, and verifies Notes removal from the registry. notes-window-feature-map State Model Window/surface modes: NotesSurfaceMode::Notes: editor/list/trash/search/action/browse overlays render inside the floating Notes host. NotesSurfaceMode::Acp: embedded Notes-hosted ACP replaces the editor body; host intercepts Escape/Cmd+K/Cmd+W before propagating to ACP. NotesViewMode::AllNotes vs NotesViewMode::Trash: active list source and available actions change. Overlay/dialog states: command bar/actions panel, note switcher/browse panel, search bar, format toolbar, confirm dialog, focus mode, ACP actions popup, ACP history popup. Notes Browse portal is a main-window AppView::NotesBrowseView { filter, selected_index } expanded two-pane portal, not the floating Notes editor. Persistent data/storage: SQLite notes table: id, title, Markdown content, timestamps, deleted state, pinned flag, sort order. SQLite note_cart_items: per-note staged context payloads with note-scoped deletion. FTS5 index/triggers for note search; fallback substring/LIKE behavior. Window bounds persisted under WindowRole::Notes, not main. Note content saves are debounced; dirty state/last-save confirmation drives footer feedback. Deleted notes are soft-deleted first; old Trash entries are pruned. Runtime caches/handles: Global Notes window handle/entity cache; cleared on close/drop. embedded_acp_chat: Option<Entity<AcpChatView>> on NotesApp, independent from ScriptListApp. notes_acp_generation: u64 rejects stale ACP actions after replacement. mention_portal_edit tracks local @note replacement sessions. history_back / history_forward, pending_focus_surface, action feedback timer, hover/focus flags, scroll handles. Notes Browse uses notes_browse_scroll_handle and reanchors selection from scroll state. Error/empty/loading states: First launch creates a welcome note if active and deleted notes are empty. Empty all-notes editor shows “No notes yet” plus create affordance. Empty Trash shows “Trash is empty” plus back-to-notes affordance. Notes Browse shows “No notes yet” for empty data and “No notes match your filter” for filtered no-match. Notes Browse search/storage errors log notes_browse_portal_load_failed and render empty rows rather than panic. Notes ACP host isolation has a known receipt gap: AcpState does not currently expose host, so host identity is proven structurally and through notes_acp_surface_opened tracing rather than getAcpState.host. notes-window-feature-map Keystrokes And Commands Shortcut/gesture: Enter Context: confirm dialog in Notes. Expected behavior: explicitly dispatches dialog Confirm because Notes uses capture-key routing and dialog focus may not be in the rendered dispatch tree yet. Edge cases: only plain Enter without platform/control confirms; must stop propagation. Shortcut/gesture: Escape Context: confirm dialog. Expected behavior: dispatches dialog Cancel and stops propagation. Edge cases: must run before editor Escape logic. Shortcut/gesture: Tab / Shift+Tab Context: confirm dialog. Expected behavior: focus next/previous dialog control. Edge cases: dialog guard must precede editor indentation logic. Shortcut/gesture: Escape Context: Notes-hosted ACP mode. Expected behavior: dismiss ACP-local popup first, then cancel active stream, then switch back to Notes editor. Edge cases: must not return to editor while attach/menu/model/history/setup popup or streaming turn consumes Escape. The test contract pins this order. notes-window-feature-map Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+K Context: Notes editor mode. Expected behavior: toggle Notes actions panel/command bar. Edge cases: if command bar/actions panel is open, close it; parent for shared actions must be stable "notes". Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+K Context: Notes-hosted ACP mode. Expected behavior: open/close Notes-hosted ACP actions dialog, refresh models before snapshot, restore ACP composer focus on close. Edge cases: dispatch uses originating weak AcpChatView plus notes_acp_generation, not current cache. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Enter Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: open embedded ACP and stage selected note/cart as inline mentions. Edge cases: claimed before general platform shortcuts; no legacy raw set_ai_input injection. notes-window-feature-map Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+A Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: send current note/cart to embedded Notes ACP. Edge cases: in ACP mode it requests ACP chat focus instead of restaging. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+W Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: close command bar/switcher, save Notes bounds, close dialogs, remove Notes window, conditionally restore launcher. Edge cases: must stop propagation; close dialogs before remove. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+W Context: Notes-hosted ACP mode. Expected behavior: save note, prepare embedded ACP for host hide, persist WindowRole::Notes bounds, close dialogs, remove window, conditionally restore launcher. Edge cases: ACP close cleanup order is pinned. notes-window-feature-map Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+N / Cmd+Shift+N Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: create empty note / create note from clipboard. Edge cases: owned by Notes; must stop propagation and auto-resize safely even when restored height exceeds default max. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+P Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle note switcher/browse panel. Edge cases: closes actions panel first; in active note mention replacement, selection should try replacing token before normal note switch. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+P Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle Markdown preview. Edge cases: preview is read mode; editor state remains source of truth. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+F Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: focus editor and dispatch window-local Search for find-in-note. Edge cases: must route through the Notes window so other app windows do not steal search. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+F Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle Notes search field across notes. Edge cases: search refresh logs start/completion/failure; clearing search reloads all notes. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+T Context: Notes editor/trash. Expected behavior: toggle All Notes ↔ Trash. Edge cases: Escape from Trash returns to All Notes before closing window. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Z Context: Trash view with selected note. Expected behavior: restore selected note. Edge cases: no-op outside Trash. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Backspace / Cmd+Shift+Backspace / Cmd+Shift+Delete as exposed by code/tests. Context: selected note. Expected behavior: route through delete confirmation helper. Edge cases: must not silently swallow in Trash; if helper declines, propagate. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+D Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: duplicate selected note. Edge cases: duplicate feedback set before selecting duplicate. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+D Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: current keyboard branch inserts date/time; action metadata also advertises copy deeplink as shift+cmd+d. Edge cases: possible shortcut/display conflict; see Open Questions. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+C Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: copy as Markdown. Edge cases: feedback must notify after state update. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+L Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle checklist on current line. Edge cases: preserves cursor and marks note dirty. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+L Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: select current line. Edge cases: must stop propagation. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+B, Cmd+I, Cmd+E Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: insert bold, italic, inline-code Markdown wrappers. Edge cases: formatting replacement must wrap selected text and leave cursor inside empty wrappers. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+I Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle pin state on current note. Edge cases: resort list and footer feedback. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+H, Cmd+Shift+-, Cmd+Shift+., Cmd+Shift+X, Cmd+Shift+U Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: cycle heading, insert horizontal rule, blockquote, strikethrough, transform case. Edge cases: mark note dirty; stop propagation. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+J Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: join lines. Edge cases: must not conflict with ACP/portal mode. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+V Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: smart paste if transformation succeeds. Edge cases: if smart paste declines, allow normal paste. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Up / Cmd+Down Context: Notes editor when editor is not focused. Expected behavior: select previous/next note. Edge cases: when editor is focused, do not steal normal cursor movement. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+Up / Cmd+Shift+Down Context: Notes editor when editor is not focused. Expected behavior: jump first/last note. Edge cases: same editor-focus guard. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+[ / Cmd+] Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: navigate note history back/forward. Edge cases: supports named bracketleft/bracketright keys. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+1 … Cmd+9 Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: select pinned note by ordinal. Edge cases: ignored with Shift; only pinned list counts. Shortcut/gesture: Tab / Shift+Tab Context: editor, no platform/control/alt. Expected behavior: indent/outdent current line. Edge cases: dialog Tab wins before this. Shortcut/gesture: Alt+Up / Alt+Down, Alt+Shift+Up / Alt+Shift+Down Context: editor. Expected behavior: move current line up/down; duplicate line up/down with Shift. Edge cases: marks note dirty. Shortcut/gesture: Ctrl+Shift+K Context: editor. Expected behavior: delete current line. Edge cases: not ACP actions; local editor command. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+O Context: cursor/focus on @note inline token. Expected behavior: open note switcher as replacement portal for focused note mention. Edge cases: footer advertises replace; note selection should replace active token before normal switch. Shortcut/gesture: arrow keys / wheel / click / double-click Context: Notes Browse portal. Expected behavior: Up/Down changes selected note and preview; wheel reanchors selection; click selects; second click/double-click can submit attach in portal mode. Edge cases: selection and preview must stay synchronized; scroll logs use notes_browse. Scenarios Scenario name: Open Notes as independent floating host Start state: launcher may be visible/hidden; Notes closed. Steps: trigger Notes open. Expected result: Notes window registers as kind:"notes", semanticSurface:"notes", has its own focus/window handle, and does not alias main. Verification signal: listAutomationWindows/resolver returns Notes by kind/title; tests/automation/notes_window_targeting.rs. Scenario name: Root note row opens existing Notes host Start state: main launcher shows a Note row; Notes may already be open. Steps: activate row. Expected result: open_note_in_notes_window focuses/selects note without toggling an already-open Notes window closed. Verification signal: source audit against lat.md/notes.md#Host Contract. Scenario name: Create/edit/autosave note Start state: Notes editor active. Steps: Cmd+N, type Markdown, wait debounce. Expected result: note content/title updates; dirty marker then saved check; auto-resize runs if line count changes. Verification signal: storage row updated; footer has_unsaved_changes/saved feedback; no inverted clamp when restored height > max. Scenario name: Create note from clipboard Start state: Notes editor active with clipboard content. Steps: Cmd+Shift+N. Expected result: new note seeded from clipboard; shortcut consumed by Notes. Verification signal: new note appears in notes table and selected editor content. Scenario name: Search and switch notes Start state: multiple active notes. Steps: Cmd+P, type filter, arrow/select/Enter. Expected result: note switcher filters Pinned/Recent actions, highlights current note, switches selected note or replaces active @note token if replacement session exists. Verification signal: selected note id/editor value changes; get_note_switcher_actions sections and empty fallback. Scenario name: Find within current note Start state: note selected. Steps: Cmd+F, search text. Expected result: Notes window-local Search opens; other app windows do not receive find. Verification signal: source check for window.dispatch_action(Box::new(Search), cx). Scenario name: Cross-note search Start state: Notes editor active. Steps: Cmd+Shift+F, type query. Expected result: visible notes are storage-backed search results; clear query reloads all notes; failures log and do not silently swallow. Verification signal: notes_search_refresh_started/completed/failed logs. Scenario name: Trash flow Start state: selected active note. Steps: delete shortcut/command, confirm; Cmd+Shift+T; Cmd+Z; permanent delete from Trash. Expected result: soft-delete first, Trash view can restore, permanent delete removes row. Verification signal: deleted_at changes; confirm logs; Trash empty/restore state. Scenario name: Send selected note/cart to Notes-hosted ACP Start state: selected note, optional note cart items. Steps: Cmd+Enter or Cmd+Shift+A. Expected result: embedded ACP opens inside Notes; note/cart context becomes inline mention chips; duplicate cart items dedupe; consumed rows deleted only after successful staging. Verification signal: getAcpState targeted to Notes shows staged chips; logs include acp_host_inline_context_staged; agentic notes-embedded-acp-context-cart.ts asserts one deduped chip and zero cart rows after handoff. notes-window-feature-map Scenario name: Reuse embedded ACP without overwriting draft Start state: Notes ACP open with draft text. Steps: close/return to editor, reopen ACP. Expected result: reused view preserves draft; reuse path does not call generic set_input. Verification signal: agentic draft replay sets " draft with spaces " and verifies byte-exact input after reuse. notes-window-feature-map Scenario name: Agent switch from Notes ACP actions Start state: Notes-hosted ACP with draft/context. Steps: Cmd+K, choose Change Agent. Expected result: popup refreshes models before snapshot, captures originating view/generation, persists new agent, drops/relaunches view, restores draft snapshot. Verification signal: notes_acp_actions_parity_contract, notes-acp-actions-originating-view.ts, logs acp_refresh_models_requested, notes_acp_switch_agent_relaunched. Scenario name: ACP Escape ordering Start state: Notes-hosted ACP with popup or stream or idle. Steps: press Escape repeatedly. Expected result: popup dismissed first; stream cancelled second; idle then returns to editor. Verification signal: notes_acp_escape_dismissed_local_popup, notes_acp_escape_cancelled_streaming, surface mode returns to Notes only when idle. Scenario name: ACP history from Notes host Start state: Notes-hosted ACP active. Steps: open history via ACP action/command/@history. Expected result: Notes-anchored local history popup opens; only AcpHistory portal is allowed; unsupported portal kinds cancel staged session. Verification signal: tests/notes_acp_history_portal_terminal_contract.rs; handle_acp_portal_static cancellation checks. Scenario name: Notes Browse attach/cancel Start state: ACP attachment portal requests Notes Browse. Steps: filter notes, arrow/wheel/click, Enter; or Escape. Expected result: Enter attaches FocusedTarget with stable note semantic id; Escape cancels portal before clearing filter; Cmd+W cancels portal and closes main. Verification signal: getAcpState pending context; source contract for Escape ordering and stable semantic ID. Scenario name: Close Notes while ACP active Start state: Notes ACP mode. Steps: Cmd+W. Expected result: save, prepare_for_host_hide, close actions/dialogs, save WindowRole::Notes, remove Notes, conditional launcher restore. Verification signal: source contract ordering; no orphaned actions or dialogs. Visual States State: Floating Notes editor, active notes What is visible: custom Notes titlebar/chrome, Markdown editor, optional footer metadata, selected note stats, note position, relative time, sort/trash/auto-size indicators. Focus owner: editor input by default unless actions/browse/dialog owns focus. Footer/actions/chrome: hover/focus mode can fade chrome; footer shows word/char stats, cursor line, selection stats, saved/dirty feedback, sort/trash controls. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: kind:"notes", semanticSurface:"notes", stable title “Script Kit Notes”. State: Empty active notes What is visible: “No notes yet”, “Create your first note”, Cmd+N / Cmd+Shift+N hints. Focus owner: Notes root/editor focus handle. Footer/actions/chrome: create affordance. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target still resolvable. State: Trash view What is visible: deleted notes or “Trash is empty”; back-to-notes affordance. Focus owner: Notes root/editor or dialog depending delete/restore flow. Footer/actions/chrome: restore/delete permanently/empty trash/back to notes affordances; Cmd+Z restore. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target. State: Search bar What is visible: search input and match counter. Focus owner: search_state. Footer/actions/chrome: note list/search results affect position counters. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target with search-visible state. State: Markdown preview What is visible: rendered Markdown blocks, headings, lists, code fences with syntax highlighting. Focus owner: Notes root/editor host, not editable text. Footer/actions/chrome: mode indicator MD. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: notes-markdown-preview. State: Focus mode What is visible: editor with hidden/faded titlebar/footer/toolbar. Focus owner: editor. Footer/actions/chrome: chrome opacity suppressed unless hovered. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target. State: Notes actions panel / command bar What is visible: modal overlay/searchable command list: New, Duplicate, Browse, Find, Copy Markdown, Deeplink, Quicklink, Export/HTML, Send to Agent Chat, Trash actions, Enable Auto-Sizing. Focus owner: command bar/actions panel. Footer/actions/chrome: backdrop closes; Cmd+K/Escape close; rows filtered by selection/trash/auto-size state. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: parent automation id must be "notes". State: Note switcher / browse panel What is visible: searchable note rows grouped Pinned/Recent, current note marked •, pinned icon, preview/relative-time descriptions, empty “No notes yet”. Focus owner: note switcher dialog. Footer/actions/chrome: Escape/backdrop closes. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target; replacement mode may title context “Replace @note”. State: Confirm dialog What is visible: delete/permanent-delete confirmation. Focus owner: dialog. Footer/actions/chrome: Enter confirms, Escape cancels, Tab cycles. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: confirm popup layer; Notes keyboard explicitly routes Confirm/Cancel. State: Notes-hosted ACP What is visible: embedded Agent Chat inside Notes, external ACP footer below chat. Focus owner: embedded AcpChatView focus handle. Footer/actions/chrome: shared external footer labels/order; Cmd+K Actions; host close returns to editor. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: target {kind:"notes"} for Notes-hosted ACP state; no separate host field in AcpState yet. State: Notes ACP actions popup What is visible: shared ACP actions dialog chrome, model/agent/history actions filtered for Notes host. Focus owner: actions popup while open; ACP composer restored after close. Footer/actions/chrome: parent automation id "notes"; close via host helper. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: actions popup parented to Notes; stale dispatch rejected by generation. State: Notes ACP history popup What is visible: local AcpHistory rows/query popup anchored to Notes. Focus owner: history popup; composer restored on accept/cancel. Footer/actions/chrome: only history portal is locally allowed. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes-hosted ACP history uses originating view. State: Notes Browse expanded portal What is visible: header filter input plus note count, left note list, right preview pane, footer hints. Focus owner: main-window shared input/focus handle for notes_browse. Footer/actions/chrome: portal footer shows ↵ Attach Note + Esc Cancel; non-portal footer shows Esc Back; expanded scaffold with preview panel. notes-window-feature-map Accessibility/automation target if applicable: AppView::NotesBrowseView; note target semantic id generated from note id, not display index. Invariants And Regression Risks Invariant: Notes is a separate floating host, not a launcher panel clone. Why it matters: prevents main-window hide/focus/surface transitions from accidentally hiding or mutating Notes. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md, src/notes/window/window_ops.rs, tests/automation/notes_window_targeting.rs. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes and main launcher have distinct embedded_acp_chat fields. Why it matters: host isolation; Notes ACP cannot inherit/mutate main ACP state. Files/tests that pin it: tests/notes_hosted_acp_host_isolation_contract.rs. Invariant: ensure_embedded_acp_view reuses cached ACP without overwriting composer; explicit relaunch uses draft snapshots. Why it matters: reuse and replacement are different user intents. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, tests/notes_acp_agent_switch_draft_contract.rs, scripts/agentic/notes-acp-draft-agent-switch-replay.ts. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes-hosted ACP only advertises/hosts AcpHistory. Why it matters: File/Clipboard/main-panel portals cannot return to the floating Notes host. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md, src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, tests/notes_ai_routing.rs, tests/notes_acp_history_portal_terminal_contract.rs. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes ACP Escape order is popup → cancel stream → editor. Why it matters: prevents losing active ACP work or closing the surface before local state consumes Escape. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/keyboard.rs, tests/notes_acp_escape_cmdw_contract.rs. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes ACP Cmd+W prepares ACP before removing the Notes window. Why it matters: prevents orphaned ACP popup state/actions and persists correct bounds. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/keyboard.rs, src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, tests/notes_acp_escape_cmdw_contract.rs. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes ACP actions dispatch to originating weak view plus notes_acp_generation. Why it matters: delayed popup actions must not mutate a replacement ACP thread. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, tests/notes_acp_actions_parity_contract.rs, scripts/agentic/notes-acp-actions-originating-view.ts. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes actions popups use parent automation id "notes". Why it matters: popup auto-close/focus should use Notes key-window checks, not main focus. Files/tests that pin it: tests/automation/notes_window_targeting.rs, src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, src/actions/command_bar.rs. Invariant: Note-cart handoff dedupes, stages replacement context, and deletes note-scoped ids only after successful staging. Why it matters: no stale chips, duplicate chips, or cross-note cart deletion. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md#ACP staging replacement, tests/notes_context_cart_staging_contract.rs, src/notes/storage.rs, scripts/agentic/notes-embedded-acp-context-cart.ts. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: note switch clears host-owned ACP context for previous note. Why it matters: hidden embedded ACP cannot keep stale note chips. Files/tests that pin it: tests/notes_context_cart_staging_contract.rs. Invariant: Notes Browse target identity uses note id, not display index. Why it matters: filter/sort changes cannot alter attached target identity. Files/tests that pin it: src/render_builtins/notes_browse.rs, tests/notes_browse_surface_contract.rs. Invariant: Notes Browse Escape cancels attachment portal before clearing filter. Why it matters: cancel must restore ACP portal state instead of mutating browse filter first. Files/tests that pin it: tests/notes_browse_surface_contract.rs; key handler lines show portal cancel before filter clear. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes Browse selection, preview, wheel, click, and scroll handle stay synchronized. Why it matters: attaching must use the visible selected row, not stale index. Files/tests that pin it: src/render_builtins/notes_browse.rs, tests/notes_browse_surface_contract.rs. Invariant: Notes opts out of app-level hide with setCanHide:false. Why it matters: hiding the launcher must not hide Notes. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md, src/notes/window/window_ops.rs, src/notes/window/tests.rs. Invariant: Notes close path releases global locks before updating/removing window and removes both automation/runtime registrations. Why it matters: avoids double-lease/deadlock and stale automation entries. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md#Host Contract. Invariant: Markdown editor disables dynamic bottom margin. Why it matters: deleting trailing lines should collapse scroll extent instead of leaving half-window blank space. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/init.rs, src/notes/window/tests.rs. Invariant: auto-resize treats restored height as valid lower bound. Why it matters: note creation cannot panic on clamp(min > max). Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/init.rs, src/notes/window/tests.rs. Invariant: behavior/architecture/test changes require lat.md update and lat check. Why it matters: Notes contracts live in the repo knowledge graph and are source-linked. Files/tests that pin it: AGENTS.md, .agents/skills/notes-window/SKILL.md, lat.md/tests/notes-acp.md. Note-cart ACP handoff: run bun scripts/agentic/notes-embedded-acp-context-cart.ts; prove duplicate cart rows produce one ACP chip and are consumed after staging. ACP draft reuse: run bun scripts/agentic/notes-acp-draft-agent-switch-replay.ts; prove byte-exact draft survives reuse. Native input/OS focus proof only when AppKit key-window, setCanHide:false, traffic-light close, or Accessibility focus is the suspected regression. For normal behavior, state receipts/logs should be enough; screenshots are not the default. Open Questions / Gaps Gap: AcpState has no explicit host:"notes" field. Why it matters: live proof of Notes-hosted ACP identity must currently infer host via automation target, structural isolation, and notes_acp_surface_opened logs. Suggested next check: add or validate a host field/receipt if future automation consumers need direct host attribution. Gap: possible Cmd+Shift+D conflict. Why it matters: NotesAction::CopyDeeplink advertises shift+cmd+d, while the keyboard branch shown in the bundle routes Cmd+Shift+D to insert_date_time; this could confuse users and tests. Suggested next check: verify live behavior and decide whether direct shortcut or action hint is canonical. Gap: Notes Browse portal is main-window hosted, while Notes editor browse panel is floating-Notes hosted. Why it matters: agents can confuse Cmd+P note switcher with AppView::NotesBrowseView attachment portal. Why it matters: implementation agents need that adjacent portal spec to reason about pending portal survival/cancel semantics. Why it matters: command names may differ if the file is included by a parent tests/automation harness.
