Answer:

006 Notes Window / Notes Browse / Notes-hosted ACP Boundaries Owns: Dedicated floating NotesApp host: editor state, note list/trash modes, Notes window bounds, hover/focus/chrome, local actions UI, local note switcher, Markdown editor/preview, autosave, auto-resize, clipboard/export/deeplink/quicklink, soft-delete/restore/permanent-delete flows. Notes-hosted ACP: opening/reusing embedded AcpChatView, Notes-owned ACP callbacks, Notes ACP footer host, Notes ACP actions popup, Notes ACP history popup, Notes-specific ACP close/focus behavior, note-cart handoff, note-target staging, stale-hosted-context cleanup, draft snapshot restore across agent switch. Notes Browse expanded attachment portal surface in src/render_builtins/notes_browse.rs: searchable active-note list, preview pane, note attach target construction, selection/scroll synchronization, portal cancel/attach semantics. Notes automation identity: AutomationWindowKind::Notes, stable id="notes" parent for actions, semanticSurface:"notes", targeted getState/getElements/waitFor/batch behavior. lat.md/notes.md and lat.md/tests/notes-acp.md contracts for Notes behavior, architecture, and tests. Does not own: Main launcher ACP cache, main-panel ACP surface placement, detached ACP popup lifecycle, generic AcpChatView composer internals except where Notes host callbacks/staging require host-specific contracts. Generic attachment portal machinery, File/Clipboard/Browser/Dictation portals, generic actions-popup implementation, generic command-bar/action registry behavior outside the Notes parent/focus contract. Root unified Notes search ranking/opening except the boundary that root note rows must use open_note_in_notes_window, not the toggle-open helper. Quick Terminal / PTY harness flows. Adjacent feature dependencies: $acp-chat-core: ACP lifecycle, footer, actions, model/agent/session behavior. $acp-context-composer: inline context chips, @history, pending portal sessions, pasted/mention token state. $actions-popups: shared ACP actions dialog chrome, parented actions windows, close/focus behavior. $protocol-automation: Notes-targeted getState, getElements, waitFor, batch, automation registry identity. $agentic-testing: state-first runtime receipts and cleanup. $platform-windowing-macos: floating panel, setCanHide:false, AppKit focus/hide independence. $lat-md: lat.md updates plus lat check whenever behavior/contracts/tests change. Notes is explicitly documented as a separate floating host with its own editor state, actions UI, list/trash modes, and reusable embedded ACP surface. notes-window-feature-map User Stories As a user, I can open Notes as a separate floating window that does not behave like a launcher panel clone. As a user, I can create a new note, create a note from clipboard, type Markdown, preview Markdown, use formatting helpers, and rely on debounced save. As a user, I can browse/switch notes, search within the current note, search across notes, pin notes, jump through note history, and sort notes. As a user, I can delete notes into Trash, view Trash, restore notes, permanently delete notes, and empty Trash. As a user, I can copy a note as Markdown, copy a deeplink, create a Markdown quicklink, and copy/export HTML-style output. As a user, I can send the current note/selection/cart to Agent Chat inside the Notes window without opening the main launcher ACP. As a user, I can switch between Notes editor mode and Notes-hosted ACP mode while keeping the embedded ACP conversation/draft when reuse is intended. As a user, I can open Notes-hosted ACP actions, change agent/model/history, and have actions apply to the originating embedded ACP view rather than a replaced/stale view. As a user, I can open local ACP History from Notes-hosted ACP and attach/cancel through the same staged replacement contract used elsewhere. As a user, I can use Notes Browse as an attachment portal to search active notes, preview content, attach a selected note, or cancel cleanly. As an automation user, I can target Notes as {kind:"notes"} and not accidentally hit the main window. The targeting test registers main and Notes separately, resolves Notes by kind/title, and verifies Notes removal from the registry. notes-window-feature-map State Model Window/surface modes: NotesSurfaceMode::Notes: editor/list/trash/search/action/browse overlays render inside the floating Notes host. NotesSurfaceMode::Acp: embedded Notes-hosted ACP replaces the editor body; host intercepts Escape/Cmd+K/Cmd+W before propagating to ACP. NotesViewMode::AllNotes vs NotesViewMode::Trash: active list source and available actions change. Overlay/dialog states: command bar/actions panel, note switcher/browse panel, search bar, format toolbar, confirm dialog, focus mode, ACP actions popup, ACP history popup. Notes Browse portal is a main-window AppView::NotesBrowseView { filter, selected_index } expanded two-pane portal, not the floating Notes editor. Persistent data/storage: SQLite notes table: id, title, Markdown content, timestamps, deleted state, pinned flag, sort order. SQLite note_cart_items: per-note staged context payloads with note-scoped deletion. FTS5 index/triggers for note search; fallback substring/LIKE behavior. Window bounds persisted under WindowRole::Notes, not main. Note content saves are debounced; dirty state/last-save confirmation drives footer feedback. Deleted notes are soft-deleted first; old Trash entries are pruned. Runtime caches/handles: Global Notes window handle/entity cache; cleared on close/drop. embedded_acp_chat: Option<Entity<AcpChatView>> on NotesApp, independent from ScriptListApp. notes_acp_generation: u64 rejects stale ACP actions after replacement. mention_portal_edit tracks local @note replacement sessions. history_back / history_forward, pending_focus_surface, action feedback timer, hover/focus flags, scroll handles. Notes Browse uses notes_browse_scroll_handle and reanchors selection from scroll state. Error/empty/loading states: First launch creates a welcome note if active and deleted notes are empty. Empty all-notes editor shows “No notes yet” plus create affordance. Empty Trash shows “Trash is empty” plus back-to-notes affordance. Notes Browse shows “No notes yet” for empty data and “No notes match your filter” for filtered no-match. Notes Browse search/storage errors log notes_browse_portal_load_failed and render empty rows rather than panic. Notes ACP host isolation has a known receipt gap: AcpState does not currently expose host, so host identity is proven structurally and through notes_acp_surface_opened tracing rather than getAcpState.host. notes-window-feature-map Keystrokes And Commands Shortcut/gesture: Enter Context: confirm dialog in Notes. Expected behavior: explicitly dispatches dialog Confirm because Notes uses capture-key routing and dialog focus may not be in the rendered dispatch tree yet. Edge cases: only plain Enter without platform/control confirms; must stop propagation. Shortcut/gesture: Escape Context: confirm dialog. Expected behavior: dispatches dialog Cancel and stops propagation. Edge cases: must run before editor Escape logic. Shortcut/gesture: Tab / Shift+Tab Context: confirm dialog. Expected behavior: focus next/previous dialog control. Edge cases: dialog guard must precede editor indentation logic. Shortcut/gesture: Escape Context: Notes-hosted ACP mode. Expected behavior: dismiss ACP-local popup first, then cancel active stream, then switch back to Notes editor. Edge cases: must not return to editor while attach/menu/model/history/setup popup or streaming turn consumes Escape. The test contract pins this order. notes-window-feature-map Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+K Context: Notes editor mode. Expected behavior: toggle Notes actions panel/command bar. Edge cases: if command bar/actions panel is open, close it; parent for shared actions must be stable "notes". Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+K Context: Notes-hosted ACP mode. Expected behavior: open/close Notes-hosted ACP actions dialog, refresh models before snapshot, restore ACP composer focus on close. Edge cases: dispatch uses originating weak AcpChatView plus notes_acp_generation, not current cache. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Enter Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: open embedded ACP and stage selected note/cart as inline mentions. Edge cases: claimed before general platform shortcuts; no legacy raw set_ai_input injection. notes-window-feature-map Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+A Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: send current note/cart to embedded Notes ACP. Edge cases: in ACP mode it requests ACP chat focus instead of restaging. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+W Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: close command bar/switcher, save Notes bounds, close dialogs, remove Notes window, conditionally restore launcher. Edge cases: must stop propagation; close dialogs before remove. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+W Context: Notes-hosted ACP mode. Expected behavior: save note, prepare embedded ACP for host hide, persist WindowRole::Notes bounds, close dialogs, remove window, conditionally restore launcher. Edge cases: ACP close cleanup order is pinned. notes-window-feature-map Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+N / Cmd+Shift+N Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: create empty note / create note from clipboard. Edge cases: owned by Notes; must stop propagation and auto-resize safely even when restored height exceeds default max. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+P Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle note switcher/browse panel. Edge cases: closes actions panel first; in active note mention replacement, selection should try replacing token before normal note switch. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+P Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle Markdown preview. Edge cases: preview is read mode; editor state remains source of truth. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+F Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: focus editor and dispatch window-local Search for find-in-note. Edge cases: must route through the Notes window so other app windows do not steal search. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+F Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle Notes search field across notes. Edge cases: search refresh logs start/completion/failure; clearing search reloads all notes. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+T Context: Notes editor/trash. Expected behavior: toggle All Notes ↔ Trash. Edge cases: Escape from Trash returns to All Notes before closing window. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Z Context: Trash view with selected note. Expected behavior: restore selected note. Edge cases: no-op outside Trash. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Backspace / Cmd+Shift+Backspace / Cmd+Shift+Delete as exposed by code/tests. Context: selected note. Expected behavior: route through delete confirmation helper. Edge cases: must not silently swallow in Trash; if helper declines, propagate. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+D Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: duplicate selected note. Edge cases: duplicate feedback set before selecting duplicate. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+D Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: current keyboard branch inserts date/time; action metadata also advertises copy deeplink as shift+cmd+d. Edge cases: possible shortcut/display conflict; see Open Questions. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+C Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: copy as Markdown. Edge cases: feedback must notify after state update. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+L Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle checklist on current line. Edge cases: preserves cursor and marks note dirty. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+L Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: select current line. Edge cases: must stop propagation. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+B, Cmd+I, Cmd+E Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: insert bold, italic, inline-code Markdown wrappers. Edge cases: formatting replacement must wrap selected text and leave cursor inside empty wrappers. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+I Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: toggle pin state on current note. Edge cases: resort list and footer feedback. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+H, Cmd+Shift+-, Cmd+Shift+., Cmd+Shift+X, Cmd+Shift+U Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: cycle heading, insert horizontal rule, blockquote, strikethrough, transform case. Edge cases: mark note dirty; stop propagation. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+J Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: join lines. Edge cases: must not conflict with ACP/portal mode. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+V Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: smart paste if transformation succeeds. Edge cases: if smart paste declines, allow normal paste. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Up / Cmd+Down Context: Notes editor when editor is not focused. Expected behavior: select previous/next note. Edge cases: when editor is focused, do not steal normal cursor movement. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+Up / Cmd+Shift+Down Context: Notes editor when editor is not focused. Expected behavior: jump first/last note. Edge cases: same editor-focus guard. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+[ / Cmd+] Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: navigate note history back/forward. Edge cases: supports named bracketleft/bracketright keys. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+1 … Cmd+9 Context: Notes editor. Expected behavior: select pinned note by ordinal. Edge cases: ignored with Shift; only pinned list counts. Shortcut/gesture: Tab / Shift+Tab Context: editor, no platform/control/alt. Expected behavior: indent/outdent current line. Edge cases: dialog Tab wins before this. Shortcut/gesture: Alt+Up / Alt+Down, Alt+Shift+Up / Alt+Shift+Down Context: editor. Expected behavior: move current line up/down; duplicate line up/down with Shift. Edge cases: marks note dirty. Shortcut/gesture: Ctrl+Shift+K Context: editor. Expected behavior: delete current line. Edge cases: not ACP actions; local editor command. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+Shift+O Context: cursor/focus on @note inline token. Expected behavior: open note switcher as replacement portal for focused note mention. Edge cases: footer advertises replace; note selection should replace active token before normal switch. Shortcut/gesture: arrow keys / wheel / click / double-click Context: Notes Browse portal. Expected behavior: Up/Down changes selected note and preview; wheel reanchors selection; click selects; second click/double-click can submit attach in portal mode. Edge cases: selection and preview must stay synchronized; scroll logs use notes_browse. Scenarios Scenario name: Open Notes as independent floating host Start state: launcher may be visible/hidden; Notes closed. Steps: trigger Notes open. Expected result: Notes window registers as kind:"notes", semanticSurface:"notes", has its own focus/window handle, and does not alias main. Verification signal: listAutomationWindows/resolver returns Notes by kind/title; tests/automation/notes_window_targeting.rs. Scenario name: Root note row opens existing Notes host Start state: main launcher shows a Note row; Notes may already be open. Steps: activate row. Expected result: open_note_in_notes_window focuses/selects note without toggling an already-open Notes window closed. Verification signal: source audit against lat.md/notes.md#Host Contract. Scenario name: Create/edit/autosave note Start state: Notes editor active. Steps: Cmd+N, type Markdown, wait debounce. Expected result: note content/title updates; dirty marker then saved check; auto-resize runs if line count changes. Verification signal: storage row updated; footer has_unsaved_changes/saved feedback; no inverted clamp when restored height > max. Scenario name: Create note from clipboard Start state: Notes editor active with clipboard content. Steps: Cmd+Shift+N. Expected result: new note seeded from clipboard; shortcut consumed by Notes. Verification signal: new note appears in notes table and selected editor content. Scenario name: Search and switch notes Start state: multiple active notes. Steps: Cmd+P, type filter, arrow/select/Enter. Expected result: note switcher filters Pinned/Recent actions, highlights current note, switches selected note or replaces active @note token if replacement session exists. Verification signal: selected note id/editor value changes; get_note_switcher_actions sections and empty fallback. Scenario name: Find within current note Start state: note selected. Steps: Cmd+F, search text. Expected result: Notes window-local Search opens; other app windows do not receive find. Verification signal: source check for window.dispatch_action(Box::new(Search), cx). Scenario name: Cross-note search Start state: Notes editor active. Steps: Cmd+Shift+F, type query. Expected result: visible notes are storage-backed search results; clear query reloads all notes; failures log and do not silently swallow. Verification signal: notes_search_refresh_started/completed/failed logs. Scenario name: Trash flow Start state: selected active note. Steps: delete shortcut/command, confirm; Cmd+Shift+T; Cmd+Z; permanent delete from Trash. Expected result: soft-delete first, Trash view can restore, permanent delete removes row. Verification signal: deleted_at changes; confirm logs; Trash empty/restore state. Scenario name: Send selected note/cart to Notes-hosted ACP Start state: selected note, optional note cart items. Steps: Cmd+Enter or Cmd+Shift+A. Expected result: embedded ACP opens inside Notes; note/cart context becomes inline mention chips; duplicate cart items dedupe; consumed rows deleted only after successful staging. Verification signal: getAcpState targeted to Notes shows staged chips; logs include acp_host_inline_context_staged; agentic notes-embedded-acp-context-cart.ts asserts one deduped chip and zero cart rows after handoff. notes-window-feature-map Scenario name: Reuse embedded ACP without overwriting draft Start state: Notes ACP open with draft text. Steps: close/return to editor, reopen ACP. Expected result: reused view preserves draft; reuse path does not call generic set_input. Verification signal: agentic draft replay sets " draft with spaces " and verifies byte-exact input after reuse. notes-window-feature-map Scenario name: Agent switch from Notes ACP actions Start state: Notes-hosted ACP with draft/context. Steps: Cmd+K, choose Change Agent. Expected result: popup refreshes models before snapshot, captures originating view/generation, persists new agent, drops/relaunches view, restores draft snapshot. Verification signal: notes_acp_actions_parity_contract, notes-acp-actions-originating-view.ts, logs acp_refresh_models_requested, notes_acp_switch_agent_relaunched. Scenario name: ACP Escape ordering Start state: Notes-hosted ACP with popup or stream or idle. Steps: press Escape repeatedly. Expected result: popup dismissed first; stream cancelled second; idle then returns to editor. Verification signal: notes_acp_escape_dismissed_local_popup, notes_acp_escape_cancelled_streaming, surface mode returns to Notes only when idle. Scenario name: ACP history from Notes host Start state: Notes-hosted ACP active. Steps: open history via ACP action/command/@history. Expected result: Notes-anchored local history popup opens; only AcpHistory portal is allowed; unsupported portal kinds cancel staged session. Verification signal: tests/notes_acp_history_portal_terminal_contract.rs; handle_acp_portal_static cancellation checks. Scenario name: Notes Browse attach/cancel Start state: ACP attachment portal requests Notes Browse. Steps: filter notes, arrow/wheel/click, Enter; or Escape. Expected result: Enter attaches FocusedTarget with stable note semantic id; Escape cancels portal before clearing filter; Cmd+W cancels portal and closes main. Verification signal: getAcpState pending context; source contract for Escape ordering and stable semantic ID. Scenario name: Close Notes while ACP active Start state: Notes ACP mode. Steps: Cmd+W. Expected result: save, prepare_for_host_hide, close actions/dialogs, save WindowRole::Notes, remove Notes, conditional launcher restore. Verification signal: source contract ordering; no orphaned actions or dialogs. Visual States State: Floating Notes editor, active notes What is visible: custom Notes titlebar/chrome, Markdown editor, optional footer metadata, selected note stats, note position, relative time, sort/trash/auto-size indicators. Focus owner: editor input by default unless actions/browse/dialog owns focus. Footer/actions/chrome: hover/focus mode can fade chrome; footer shows word/char stats, cursor line, selection stats, saved/dirty feedback, sort/trash controls. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: kind:"notes", semanticSurface:"notes", stable title “Script Kit Notes”. State: Empty active notes What is visible: “No notes yet”, “Create your first note”, Cmd+N / Cmd+Shift+N hints. Focus owner: Notes root/editor focus handle. Footer/actions/chrome: create affordance. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target still resolvable. State: Trash view What is visible: deleted notes or “Trash is empty”; back-to-notes affordance. Focus owner: Notes root/editor or dialog depending delete/restore flow. Footer/actions/chrome: restore/delete permanently/empty trash/back to notes affordances; Cmd+Z restore. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target. State: Search bar What is visible: search input and match counter. Focus owner: search_state. Footer/actions/chrome: note list/search results affect position counters. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target with search-visible state. State: Markdown preview What is visible: rendered Markdown blocks, headings, lists, code fences with syntax highlighting. Focus owner: Notes root/editor host, not editable text. Footer/actions/chrome: mode indicator MD. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: notes-markdown-preview. State: Focus mode What is visible: editor with hidden/faded titlebar/footer/toolbar. Focus owner: editor. Footer/actions/chrome: chrome opacity suppressed unless hovered. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target. State: Notes actions panel / command bar What is visible: modal overlay/searchable command list: New, Duplicate, Browse, Find, Copy Markdown, Deeplink, Quicklink, Export/HTML, Send to Agent Chat, Trash actions, Enable Auto-Sizing. Focus owner: command bar/actions panel. Footer/actions/chrome: backdrop closes; Cmd+K/Escape close; rows filtered by selection/trash/auto-size state. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: parent automation id must be "notes". State: Note switcher / browse panel What is visible: searchable note rows grouped Pinned/Recent, current note marked •, pinned icon, preview/relative-time descriptions, empty “No notes yet”. Focus owner: note switcher dialog. Footer/actions/chrome: Escape/backdrop closes. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes target; replacement mode may title context “Replace @note”. State: Confirm dialog What is visible: delete/permanent-delete confirmation. Focus owner: dialog. Footer/actions/chrome: Enter confirms, Escape cancels, Tab cycles. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: confirm popup layer; Notes keyboard explicitly routes Confirm/Cancel. State: Notes-hosted ACP What is visible: embedded Agent Chat inside Notes, external ACP footer below chat. Focus owner: embedded AcpChatView focus handle. Footer/actions/chrome: shared external footer labels/order; Cmd+K Actions; host close returns to editor. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: target {kind:"notes"} for Notes-hosted ACP state; no separate host field in AcpState yet. State: Notes ACP actions popup What is visible: shared ACP actions dialog chrome, model/agent/history actions filtered for Notes host. Focus owner: actions popup while open; ACP composer restored after close. Footer/actions/chrome: parent automation id "notes"; close via host helper. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: actions popup parented to Notes; stale dispatch rejected by generation. State: Notes ACP history popup What is visible: local AcpHistory rows/query popup anchored to Notes. Focus owner: history popup; composer restored on accept/cancel. Footer/actions/chrome: only history portal is locally allowed. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes-hosted ACP history uses originating view. State: Notes Browse expanded portal What is visible: header filter input plus note count, left note list, right preview pane, footer hints. Focus owner: main-window shared input/focus handle for notes_browse. Footer/actions/chrome: portal footer shows ↵ Attach Note + Esc Cancel; non-portal footer shows Esc Back; expanded scaffold with preview panel. notes-window-feature-map Accessibility/automation target if applicable: AppView::NotesBrowseView; note target semantic id generated from note id, not display index. Invariants And Regression Risks Invariant: Notes is a separate floating host, not a launcher panel clone. Why it matters: prevents main-window hide/focus/surface transitions from accidentally hiding or mutating Notes. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md, src/notes/window/window_ops.rs, tests/automation/notes_window_targeting.rs. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes and main launcher have distinct embedded_acp_chat fields. Why it matters: host isolation; Notes ACP cannot inherit/mutate main ACP state. Files/tests that pin it: tests/notes_hosted_acp_host_isolation_contract.rs. Invariant: ensure_embedded_acp_view reuses cached ACP without overwriting composer; explicit relaunch uses draft snapshots. Why it matters: reuse and replacement are different user intents. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, tests/notes_acp_agent_switch_draft_contract.rs, scripts/agentic/notes-acp-draft-agent-switch-replay.ts. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes-hosted ACP only advertises/hosts AcpHistory. Why it matters: File/Clipboard/main-panel portals cannot return to the floating Notes host. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md, src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, tests/notes_ai_routing.rs, tests/notes_acp_history_portal_terminal_contract.rs. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes ACP Escape order is popup → cancel stream → editor. Why it matters: prevents losing active ACP work or closing the surface before local state consumes Escape. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/keyboard.rs, tests/notes_acp_escape_cmdw_contract.rs. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes ACP Cmd+W prepares ACP before removing the Notes window. Why it matters: prevents orphaned ACP popup state/actions and persists correct bounds. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/keyboard.rs, src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, tests/notes_acp_escape_cmdw_contract.rs. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes ACP actions dispatch to originating weak view plus notes_acp_generation. Why it matters: delayed popup actions must not mutate a replacement ACP thread. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, tests/notes_acp_actions_parity_contract.rs, scripts/agentic/notes-acp-actions-originating-view.ts. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes actions popups use parent automation id "notes". Why it matters: popup auto-close/focus should use Notes key-window checks, not main focus. Files/tests that pin it: tests/automation/notes_window_targeting.rs, src/notes/window/acp_host.rs, src/actions/command_bar.rs. Invariant: Note-cart handoff dedupes, stages replacement context, and deletes note-scoped ids only after successful staging. Why it matters: no stale chips, duplicate chips, or cross-note cart deletion. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md#ACP staging replacement, tests/notes_context_cart_staging_contract.rs, src/notes/storage.rs, scripts/agentic/notes-embedded-acp-context-cart.ts. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: note switch clears host-owned ACP context for previous note. Why it matters: hidden embedded ACP cannot keep stale note chips. Files/tests that pin it: tests/notes_context_cart_staging_contract.rs. Invariant: Notes Browse target identity uses note id, not display index. Why it matters: filter/sort changes cannot alter attached target identity. Files/tests that pin it: src/render_builtins/notes_browse.rs, tests/notes_browse_surface_contract.rs. Invariant: Notes Browse Escape cancels attachment portal before clearing filter. Why it matters: cancel must restore ACP portal state instead of mutating browse filter first. Files/tests that pin it: tests/notes_browse_surface_contract.rs; key handler lines show portal cancel before filter clear. notes-window-feature-map Invariant: Notes Browse selection, preview, wheel, click, and scroll handle stay synchronized. Why it matters: attaching must use the visible selected row, not stale index. Files/tests that pin it: src/render_builtins/notes_browse.rs, tests/notes_browse_surface_contract.rs. Invariant: Notes opts out of app-level hide with setCanHide:false. Why it matters: hiding the launcher must not hide Notes. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md, src/notes/window/window_ops.rs, src/notes/window/tests.rs. Invariant: Notes close path releases global locks before updating/removing window and removes both automation/runtime registrations. Why it matters: avoids double-lease/deadlock and stale automation entries. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/notes.md#Host Contract. Invariant: Markdown editor disables dynamic bottom margin. Why it matters: deleting trailing lines should collapse scroll extent instead of leaving half-window blank space. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/init.rs, src/notes/window/tests.rs. Invariant: auto-resize treats restored height as valid lower bound. Why it matters: note creation cannot panic on clamp(min > max). Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/window/init.rs, src/notes/window/tests.rs. Invariant: behavior/architecture/test changes require lat.md update and lat check. Why it matters: Notes contracts live in the repo knowledge graph and are source-linked. Files/tests that pin it: AGENTS.md, .agents/skills/notes-window/SKILL.md, lat.md/tests/notes-acp.md. The skill proof ladder also requires the smallest falsifying proof and lat check for lattice/wiki-link changes. notes-window-feature-map Verification Map Source/static checks: cargo test --test notes_acp_agent_switch_draft_contract cargo test --test notes_acp_actions_parity_contract cargo test --test notes_acp_history_portal_terminal_contract cargo test --test notes_acp_escape_cmdw_contract cargo test --test notes_hosted_acp_host_isolation_contract cargo test --test notes_context_cart_staging_contract cargo test --test notes_browse_surface_contract cargo test --test notes_ai_routing cargo check --lib cargo fmt --check git diff --check lat check whenever lat.md, wiki links, source refs, behavior contracts, or tests change. Runtime/state-first proofs: Notes targeting: open Notes, assert listAutomationWindows/resolver sees {kind:"notes", semanticSurface:"notes"}, target {kind:"notes"} for getState, getElements, waitFor, and batch. Note-cart ACP handoff: run bun scripts/agentic/notes-embedded-acp-context-cart.ts; prove duplicate cart rows produce one ACP chip and are consumed after staging. ACP draft reuse: run bun scripts/agentic/notes-acp-draft-agent-switch-replay.ts; prove byte-exact draft survives reuse. ACP actions originating view: run bun scripts/agentic/notes-acp-actions-originating-view.ts; prove model refresh before actions popup and generation/origin checks. Escape/Cmd+W: state-first proof should sample Notes mode/ACP mode before and after simulated keys, plus logs notes_acp_escape_dismissed_local_popup, notes_acp_escape_cancelled_streaming, notes_cmd_w_close. Notes Browse portal: use getState/getElements on NotesBrowseView, simulate filter/arrow/wheel/Enter/Escape, assert selected label/preview/attached part/cancel result without screenshots. Visual/native proofs only if needed: Use screenshots only for visual acceptance: floating Notes chrome/vibrancy, Markdown preview rendering, focus-mode opacity, ACP external footer layout, Notes Browse two-pane expanded scaffold, native AppKit focus/hide behavior. Native input/OS focus proof only when AppKit key-window, setCanHide:false, traffic-light close, or Accessibility focus is the suspected regression. For normal behavior, state receipts/logs should be enough; screenshots are not the default. Open Questions / Gaps Gap: AcpState has no explicit host:"notes" field. Why it matters: live proof of Notes-hosted ACP identity must currently infer host via automation target, structural isolation, and notes_acp_surface_opened logs. Suggested next check: add or validate a host field/receipt if future automation consumers need direct host attribution. Gap: possible Cmd+Shift+D conflict. Why it matters: NotesAction::CopyDeeplink advertises shift+cmd+d, while the keyboard branch shown in the bundle routes Cmd+Shift+D to insert_date_time; this could confuse users and tests. Suggested next check: verify live behavior and decide whether direct shortcut or action hint is canonical. Gap: Notes Browse portal is main-window hosted, while Notes editor browse panel is floating-Notes hosted. Why it matters: agents can confuse Cmd+P note switcher with AppView::NotesBrowseView attachment portal. Suggested next check: ensure Feature Map 007 or adjacent portal docs clearly separate “Notes note switcher” from “Notes Browse attachment portal.” Gap: Notes ACP history portal tests cite tests/acp-portal-contract sections not included in this bundle. Why it matters: implementation agents need that adjacent portal spec to reason about pending portal survival/cancel semantics. Suggested next check: include lat.md/tests/acp-portal-contract.md in future packs when touching Notes-hosted history. Gap: exact Cargo target for tests/automation/notes_window_targeting.rs may depend on the repo’s integration-test module layout. Why it matters: command names may differ if the file is included by a parent tests/automation harness. Suggested next check: inspect Cargo.toml/test module layout before prescribing a single command in automation instructions. Suggested next feature 007 Root Unified Search Notes / Notes root rows / note deeplink open path.


<!-- Source: Oracle session root-notes-feature-map, captured 2026-05-15. -->


007 Root Unified Search Notes / Notes root rows / note deeplink open path Boundaries Owns: Root launcher SearchResult::Note / NoteMatch rows as passive launcher results, not primary fuzzy results. Grounded in the attached Feature 007 bundle. root-notes-feature-map Notes metadata search for root rows: src/notes/storage.rs#RootNotesSectionOptions, RootNoteSearchHit, root_notes_query_is_eligible, search_root_notes_meta, search_root_notes_meta_cached, search_root_notes_meta_direct. Root Notes config surface: unifiedSearch.notes.enabled, maxResults, minQueryChars, searchContent; Rust/schema/default parity through UnifiedSearchNotesConfig. Passive grouping insertion through src/scripts/grouping.rs#append_root_notes_section. Source-filter heads notes: and n: including attached text (n:meeting), spaced text (n: meeting), anywhere tokens, source-only browse (n: ), and source-filter cache isolation. Root Note selection/open path: src/app_impl/selection_fallback.rs#execute_root_note_open → crate::notes::open_note_in_notes_window(cx, note_id). Stable result identity note/{id} for root search memory/state; default action label "Open Note"; non-bindable launcher command behavior. Does not own: Full Notes editor behavior, Markdown editing, browse panel CRUD, notes cart, notes-hosted ACP, or Notes window visual internals beyond opening/focusing/selecting the note. Toggle command semantics for open_notes_window; this feature explicitly must not use that helper. Other passive sources: Files, Browser Tabs, Clipboard History, Dictation History, AI Conversations, Browser History. Primary command/script/app/window fuzzy sorting, fallback row generation, or root file handoff behavior. Generic menu syntax predicates beyond Notes source-head behavior and source-filter interaction. Adjacent feature dependencies: main-menu-search-selection: root filtering, grouped result assembly, selection resolution, row identity. notes-window: floating Notes host lifecycle and open_note_in_notes_window. builtin-filterable-surfaces: shared passive/source-filter surface conventions. protocol-automation + agentic-testing: state-first getState / getElements / waitFor proof and cleanup. theme-config-preferences: config.ts / schema / defaults parity. storage-cache-security: local SQLite / FTS / metadata-only storage boundary. User Stories As a user, I can type a normal non-empty root query and see matching Notes under a Notes passive section without those Notes outranking commands, scripts, apps, skills, windows, or actions. As a user, I can type notes: meeting, n: meeting, or n:meeting to search only Notes using the stripped query text. As a user, I can type n: / notes: to browse pinned and recently updated active notes even with no search text. As a user, I can select a root Note row and press Enter to open or focus the floating Notes window with that note selected. As a user, if the Notes window is already open, opening a root Note focuses/selects the note instead of toggling the window closed. As a user, I can find notes by title and, when searchContent is enabled, by content; root rows still expose only metadata, never note bodies. As a user, I see useful row metadata: title or Untitled Note, pinned state, relative updated time, character count, type/source as Note / Notes, and primary action Open Note. As a user, I do not see root Notes rows for ordinary empty, too-short, multiline, disabled, or advanced predicate queries unless I explicitly opt into Notes with a source head where applicable. State Model Window/surface modes: Root launcher ScriptList search mode with grouped results. Root passive result mode: SearchResult::Note classified as MainWindowPreflightResultRole::RootPassive. Source-filter active mode: RootUnifiedSourceFilterSet includes Notes; primary/disallowed sources are suppressed by shared source-filter grouping. Source-only Notes browse mode: stripped query is empty, Notes explicitly enabled, min_query_chars = 0, larger explicit-source caps applied. Floating Notes window mode: open_note_in_notes_window opens or focuses the separate Notes host and selects the note; launcher hides/resets on success. Existing Notes window mode: same helper reuses/focuses the existing handle; no toggle-close behavior. Persistent data/storage: Notes SQLite tables/FTS contain note id, title, content, timestamps, deleted state, pinned state, sort order. Root rows may use title/content FTS and LIKE fallback, but expose only id, title, updated_at, is_pinned, char_count, score. Active-only storage filter: deleted_at IS NULL. Config: UnifiedSearchNotesConfig; defaults include Notes enabled and content search enabled; clamped maxResults and minQueryChars. Runtime caches/handles: RootPassiveFrameKey includes query, advanced-query flag, source_filters, Notes options, and other passive source options. RootPassiveFrame.note_hits freezes Notes hits for the frame to avoid cross-frame drift. Ordinary root Notes search uses search_root_notes_meta_cached; cold cache warms via root-notes-search-cache and does not publish blocking results into the active frame. Explicit n: / notes: uses search_root_notes_meta_direct. ROOT_NOTES_SEARCH_CACHE_GENERATION invalidates root Notes cache on save/delete/prune. Notes window handle is owned by the Notes subsystem; root open path only calls the non-toggle note-open helper. Error/empty/loading states: Ordinary empty query: no Notes rows. Ordinary short query below minQueryChars: no Notes rows. Multiline query: no Notes rows. Advanced predicate query: no Notes passive rows. Disabled passive defaults: hidden in ordinary search; explicit positive Notes source head opts back into Notes for that query. No hits under source filter: source-filter status/no-results surface should be state-verifiable. Missing/deleted note at open time: open_note_in_notes_window errors; root path shows HUD Failed to open note and does not hide launcher. No root Notes-specific spinner is implied; cold ordinary cache is a “no rows until future warmed frame” state. Keystrokes And Commands Shortcut/gesture: Type ordinary root query, e.g. meeting Context: Main launcher root search, no source filters, Notes enabled, query eligible. Expected behavior: Matching Notes append as passive Notes section according to configured passive source order. Edge cases: Empty/short/newline/advanced/disabled queries suppress Notes; cold cache may require a later frame to show ordinary passive hits. Shortcut/gesture: Type notes: meeting or n: meeting Context: Root launcher search with explicit Notes source filter. Expected behavior: Query strips to meeting; Notes is the only allowed passive source; source caps are raised; direct search path is used. Edge cases: Disabled passive default is overridden by explicit source intent; other source rows must not bleed in. Shortcut/gesture: Type attached source query, e.g. n:meeting or notes:meeting Context: Root launcher source-filter parsing. Expected behavior: Attached text becomes stripped free text; Notes search runs for meeting. Edge cases: n:not must find Welcome to Notes through bounded LIKE fallback if FTS returns empty. Shortcut/gesture: Type source-only n: / notes: Context: Root launcher with explicit Notes source and empty stripped query. Expected behavior: Shows pinned and most recently updated active notes as browse rows. Edge cases: Verify bare n: without trailing space separately; tests explicitly pin n: . Shortcut/gesture: Press Enter on selected Note row Context: A SearchResult::Note is selected in root launcher. Expected behavior: Calls execute_root_note_open, then open_note_in_notes_window; Notes window opens/focuses, note selected, launcher hides/resets. Edge cases: Existing Notes window must not close; stale/deleted note yields HUD failure. Shortcut/gesture: Move selection to a Note row via launcher selection controls or click Context: Grouped root results include a Notes section. Expected behavior: Selected row exposes Open Note as primary action and stable key note/{id}. Edge cases: launcher_command_id remains None; row is not shortcut/alias bindable. Shortcut/gesture: Type : / source heads Context: Menu syntax discoverability. Expected behavior: Plain : can open discoverability picker; active source-filter heads such as n: should not open the power/main hint. Edge cases: Unknown heads, quoted heads, malformed tokens, processes: / p: remain non-source-filter input. Scenarios Scenario name: Ordinary eligible query appends Notes passively Start state: Launcher open; Notes enabled; active note title/content matches query; query length meets minQueryChars. Steps: Type meeting; let passive cache/frame path resolve. Expected result: Notes section appears after Files/Browser Tabs and before Clipboard History / later passive sections / fallbacks; row shows title, pinned/update/char metadata. Verification signal: getState / preflight results include role=RootPassive, source Notes, type Note, action Open Note, no content body; static: append_root_notes_section. Scenario name: Source-filter Notes query only Start state: Launcher open; active matching note exists. Steps: Type n: meeting. Expected result: computed_search_text = "meeting"; source_filters = ["Notes"]; only Notes-allowed rows/status are shown. Verification signal: main_window_preflight exposes computed_search_text, source_filters, filter_indicators; source-filter grouping suppresses disallowed sources. Scenario name: Attached Notes source query Start state: Launcher open; active note Welcome to Notes exists. Steps: Type n:not. Expected result: Free text is not; row for Welcome to Notes appears via LIKE fallback if FTS misses. Verification signal: tests/menu_syntax_source_filters.rs#source_filters_accept_attached_query_text; src/notes/storage.rs unit test_search_root_notes_meta_matches_title_substrings_when_fts_has_no_hit. Scenario name: Source-only Notes browse Start state: Launcher open; multiple active notes with pinned/recent ordering. Steps: Type n: . Expected result: Notes rows show pinned and most recently updated active notes; no note body text. Verification signal: State rows under Notes; storage query returns empty-query active metadata; source audit requires pinned/recent active metadata for n: . Scenario name: Ineligible ordinary query suppresses Notes Start state: Launcher open; Notes enabled; matching notes exist. Steps: Try empty query, too-short query, multiline query, disabled config, and advanced predicate query. Expected result: No Notes section for ordinary ineligible states. Verification signal: root_notes_query_is_eligible; grouping test root_notes_rows_do_not_append_for_empty_short_disabled_or_advanced_query. Scenario name: Active-only metadata search Start state: Matching active note and matching soft-deleted note exist. Steps: Search the token. Expected result: Only active note appears; body content is not present in row/result model. Verification signal: root_unified_notes_search_is_metadata_only_bounded_and_active_only; n.deleted_at IS NULL; RootNoteSearchHit lacks full content. Scenario name: Enter opens closed Notes window Start state: Launcher open; Notes window closed; Note row selected. Steps: Press Enter. Expected result: Floating Notes window opens; selected note is loaded; launcher hides/resets. Verification signal: State-first proof: Notes host open, selected note id/title/editor content corresponds to row; main launcher hidden. Scenario name: Enter focuses existing Notes window Start state: Floating Notes window already open; launcher has selected root Note row. Steps: Press Enter on root Note row. Expected result: Existing Notes window remains open/focused and switches/selects note; it is not toggled closed. Verification signal: Before/after window handle/open-state unchanged except focus/selection; static audit proves open_notes_window absent from execute_root_note_open. Scenario name: Stale Note open failure Start state: Root Note row exists from prior results; note is deleted before Enter. Steps: Press Enter. Expected result: HUD says Failed to open note; launcher does not hide/reset on failure. Verification signal: State/HUD receipt; open_note_in_notes_window rejects missing/deleted note. Scenario name: Passive cache/source-filter isolation Start state: Same free text can match Notes and Clipboard/Files. Steps: Search n: plan, then clipboard: plan, then unfiltered plan. Expected result: Notes hits never bleed into non-Notes source-filter frames or unfiltered frames. Verification signal: RootPassiveFrameKey.source_filters; root_unified_source_filters_contract. Scenario name: Config clamping and parity Start state: User config changes Notes root search limits. Steps: Configure Notes values outside allowed ranges. Expected result: Runtime options clamp maxResults and minQueryChars; schema/defaults stay in sync. Verification signal: root_unified_config_schema_parity_contract; UnifiedSearchConfig::notes_section_options. Visual States State: Ordinary root results with Notes section What is visible: Section header Notes; one or more Note rows; row title or Untitled Note; subtitle Pinned · Updated <relative> · <n> chars when pinned. Focus owner: Main launcher search/list; selected row if navigated. Footer/actions/chrome: Primary action Open Note; type/source tag Note / Notes. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: getElements row with result role RootPassive, source Notes, stable key note/{id}. State: Explicit Notes source filter What is visible: Notes-only filtered results or source-filter status/no-results rows; filter indicator/chip for Notes. Focus owner: Main launcher search/list. Footer/actions/chrome: Filtered root chrome; default action remains Open Note for selected Note. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: source_filters=["Notes"], computed_search_text=<stripped query>. State: Source-only Notes browse What is visible: Notes section populated by pinned/recent active notes; empty stripped query. Focus owner: Main launcher search/list. Footer/actions/chrome: Source-filter browse/status chrome. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: state rows with Notes source and metadata-only subtitles. State: Selected Note row What is visible: Highlighted Note row; title/subtitle; no note body content. Focus owner: Selected root list item. Footer/actions/chrome: Open Note; not shortcut/alias bindable. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: selected result stable key note/{id}. State: Floating Notes window after Enter What is visible: Separate Notes host; target note selected/open in editor. Focus owner: Notes window/editor, not launcher. Footer/actions/chrome: Notes window chrome; launcher hidden. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: Notes open-state/selected-note/editor-state receipt. State: Open failure HUD What is visible: Launcher remains; HUD Failed to open note. Focus owner: Launcher. Footer/actions/chrome: Existing root chrome retained. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: HUD text/state receipt. State: No eligible Notes rows What is visible: No Notes section in ordinary root; fallback/other sections may remain. Under explicit source filter, filtered no-results/status surface may be visible. Focus owner: Launcher. Footer/actions/chrome: Shared empty/filter chrome. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: no SearchResult::Note; optional source status row for explicit filter. Invariants And Regression Risks Invariant: Root Notes rows are metadata-only. Why it matters: Prevents leaking note bodies into launcher rows/state. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/storage.rs#RootNoteSearchHit; tests/source_audits/root_unified_notes_contract.rs#root_unified_notes_search_is_metadata_only_bounded_and_active_only. Invariant: Root Notes search is active-only. Why it matters: Deleted notes must not resurface from root search. Files/tests that pin it: src/notes/storage.rs SQL deleted_at IS NULL; storage unit test_search_root_notes_meta_is_bounded_active_only_and_metadata_only. Invariant: Ordinary eligibility excludes empty, short, newline, disabled, and advanced predicate queries. Why it matters: Keeps passive Notes quiet unless the query is intentional. Files/tests that pin it: root_notes_query_is_eligible; grouping test root_notes_rows_do_not_append_for_empty_short_disabled_or_advanced_query. Invariant: Explicit n: / notes: opt into Notes and source-only browse. Why it matters: User-selected source filters must work even when passive defaults are hidden. Files/tests that pin it: src/app_impl/filtering_cache.rs Notes explicit branch; tests/menu_syntax_source_filters.rs; root_unified_source_filters_contract. Invariant: Notes rows stay passive and never promote above primary rows. Why it matters: Root launcher command/script/app/window priority stays stable. Files/tests that pin it: src/scripts/grouping.rs; tests/source_audits/root_unified_passive_snapshot_contract.rs; MainWindowPreflightResultRole::RootPassive. Invariant: Passive order places Notes after Files/Browser Tabs and before Clipboard History / later passive sections / fallback rows by default. Why it matters: Section order is a user-visible navigation contract. Files/tests that pin it: append_root_notes_section; root_notes_rows_insert_after_primary_before_clipboard_acp_and_fallbacks; config passive source order parity tests. Invariant: Stable key is note/{id} but launcher command binding is None. Why it matters: Selection/history identity is stable without pretending Notes rows are bindable commands. Files/tests that pin it: src/scripts/types.rs#history_result_key; SearchResult::Note(_) => None; root_unified_notes_result_is_stable_and_non_bindable. Invariant: Enter uses open_note_in_notes_window, never toggle open_notes_window. Why it matters: Toggle helper would close an already-open Notes window. Files/tests that pin it: src/app_impl/selection_fallback.rs#execute_root_note_open; src/notes/window/window_ops.rs#open_note_in_notes_window; root_unified_notes_enter_uses_non_toggle_open_helper. Invariant: Source filters are part of passive frame keys. Why it matters: Prevents cached Notes hits from bleeding into Files, Clipboard, or unfiltered frames. Files/tests that pin it: src/main_sections/app_state.rs#RootPassiveFrameKey; src/app_impl/filtering_cache.rs#root_passive_frame_for_current_query; root_unified_source_filters_contract. Invariant: Foreground passive path is cache-only for ordinary search. Why it matters: Avoids blocking root typing on SQLite/FTS work. Files/tests that pin it: search_root_notes_meta_cached; root_unified_passive_snapshot_contract#foreground_grouping_uses_cache_only_passive_sources. Invariant: Empty FTS hits fall back to bounded LIKE search. Why it matters: Attached short source-filter queries like n:not remain useful. Files/tests that pin it: search_root_notes_meta_like; test_search_root_notes_meta_matches_title_substrings_when_fts_has_no_hit. Invariant: Config/schema/default/verification parity includes Notes. Why it matters: User-facing config cannot drift from Rust behavior or lat verification. Update lat.md/builtins.md and/or lat.md/verification.md if behavior, architecture, or verification contracts change. Gap: Bare n: / notes: without trailing space is not clearly pinned by the shown parser tests; n: is pinned. Why it matters: Users will likely type the bare source head and expect browse mode. Suggested next check: Add/confirm parser/runtime coverage for bare n: and notes: source-only browse if current parser supports it. Gap: Cold ordinary passive cache has no visible loading/refresh signal in the excerpt. Why it matters: Ordinary root Notes may not appear on the first frame, which can look flaky unless verified/understood. Suggested next check: Runtime proof for cold → warm → future-frame behavior and whether user input change/reopen is required. Gap: Exact automation field for selected note id after Notes window open is not shown. Why it matters: Enter crosses from launcher to separate Notes host; screenshot should not be needed if state exposes selected note id/editor note. Suggested next check: Confirm getState / Notes automation exposes selected note id, title, or editor content after open_note_in_notes_window. Gap: Root Note action-subject coverage exists in excerpts, but exact user-facing action menu items are not shown. Why it matters: If actions popup supports Note-specific root actions, those may belong to adjacent action features rather than Feature 007. Suggested next check: Inspect root_unified_source_actions_contract and action popup bindings before mapping non-Enter actions. Gap: Frecency/query-memory semantics are split: history_result_key returns note/{id}, while selection fallback does not record normal launcher command frecency for Note rows. Why it matters: Review agents may confuse stable row identity with bindable command/frecency behavior. Suggested next check: Confirm intended exact-query memory behavior for passive Notes rows and document it in lat.md if not already explicit. 007 Root Unified Search Notes / Notes root rows / note deeplink open path Boundaries Owns: Root launcher SearchResult::Note / NoteMatch rows as passive launcher results, not primary fuzzy results. Grounded in the attached Feature 007 bundle. root-notes-feature-map Notes metadata search for root rows: src/notes/storage.rs#RootNotesSectionOptions, RootNoteSearchHit, root_notes_query_is_eligible, search_root_notes_meta, search_root_notes_meta_cached, search_root_notes_meta_direct. Root Notes config surface: unifiedSearch.notes.enabled, maxResults, minQueryChars, searchContent; Rust/schema/default parity through UnifiedSearchNotesConfig. Passive grouping insertion through src/scripts/grouping.rs#append_root_notes_section. Source-filter heads notes: and n: including attached text (n:meeting), spaced text (n: meeting), anywhere tokens, source-only browse (n: ), and source-filter cache isolation. Root Note selection/open path: src/app_impl/selection_fallback.rs#execute_root_note_open → crate::notes::open_note_in_notes_window(cx, note_id). Stable result identity note/{id} for root search memory/state; default action label "Open Note"; non-bindable launcher command behavior. Does not own: Full Notes editor behavior, Markdown editing, browse panel CRUD, notes cart, notes-hosted ACP, or Notes window visual internals beyond opening/focusing/selecting the note. Toggle command semantics for open_notes_window; this feature explicitly must not use that helper. Other passive sources: Files, Browser Tabs, Clipboard History, Dictation History, AI Conversations, Browser History. Primary command/script/app/window fuzzy sorting, fallback row generation, or root file handoff behavior. Generic menu syntax predicates beyond Notes source-head behavior and source-filter interaction. Adjacent feature dependencies: main-menu-search-selection: root filtering, grouped result assembly, selection resolution, row identity. notes-window: floating Notes host lifecycle and open_note_in_notes_window. builtin-filterable-surfaces: shared passive/source-filter surface conventions. protocol-automation + agentic-testing: state-first getState / getElements / waitFor proof and cleanup. theme-config-preferences: config.ts / schema / defaults parity. storage-cache-security: local SQLite / FTS / metadata-only storage boundary. User Stories As a user, I can type a normal non-empty root query and see matching Notes under a Notes passive section without those Notes outranking commands, scripts, apps, skills, windows, or actions. As a user, I can type notes: meeting, n: meeting, or n:meeting to search only Notes using the stripped query text. As a user, I can type n: / notes: to browse pinned and recently updated active notes even with no search text. As a user, I can select a root Note row and press Enter to open or focus the floating Notes window with that note selected. As a user, if the Notes window is already open, opening a root Note focuses/selects the note instead of toggling the window closed. As a user, I can find notes by title and, when searchContent is enabled, by content; root rows still expose only metadata, never note bodies. As a user, I see useful row metadata: title or Untitled Note, pinned state, relative updated time, character count, type/source as Note / Notes, and primary action Open Note. As a user, I do not see root Notes rows for ordinary empty, too-short, multiline, disabled, or advanced predicate queries unless I explicitly opt into Notes with a source head where applicable. State Model Window/surface modes: Root launcher ScriptList search mode with grouped results. Root passive result mode: SearchResult::Note classified as MainWindowPreflightResultRole::RootPassive. Source-filter active mode: RootUnifiedSourceFilterSet includes Notes; primary/disallowed sources are suppressed by shared source-filter grouping. Source-only Notes browse mode: stripped query is empty, Notes explicitly enabled, min_query_chars = 0, larger explicit-source caps applied. Floating Notes window mode: open_note_in_notes_window opens or focuses the separate Notes host and selects the note; launcher hides/resets on success. Existing Notes window mode: same helper reuses/focuses the existing handle; no toggle-close behavior. Persistent data/storage: Notes SQLite tables/FTS contain note id, title, content, timestamps, deleted state, pinned state, sort order. Root rows may use title/content FTS and LIKE fallback, but expose only id, title, updated_at, is_pinned, char_count, score. Active-only storage filter: deleted_at IS NULL. Config: UnifiedSearchNotesConfig; defaults include Notes enabled and content search enabled; clamped maxResults and minQueryChars. Runtime caches/handles: RootPassiveFrameKey includes query, advanced-query flag, source_filters, Notes options, and other passive source options. RootPassiveFrame.note_hits freezes Notes hits for the frame to avoid cross-frame drift. Ordinary root Notes search uses search_root_notes_meta_cached; cold cache warms via root-notes-search-cache and does not publish blocking results into the active frame. Explicit n: / notes: uses search_root_notes_meta_direct. ROOT_NOTES_SEARCH_CACHE_GENERATION invalidates root Notes cache on save/delete/prune. Notes window handle is owned by the Notes subsystem; root open path only calls the non-toggle note-open helper. Error/empty/loading states: Ordinary empty query: no Notes rows. Ordinary short query below minQueryChars: no Notes rows. Multiline query: no Notes rows. Advanced predicate query: no Notes passive rows. Disabled passive defaults: hidden in ordinary search; explicit positive Notes source head opts back into Notes for that query. No hits under source filter: source-filter status/no-results surface should be state-verifiable. Missing/deleted note at open time: open_note_in_notes_window errors; root path shows HUD Failed to open note and does not hide launcher. No root Notes-specific spinner is implied; cold ordinary cache is a “no rows until future warmed frame” state. Keystrokes And Commands Shortcut/gesture: Type ordinary root query, e.g. meeting Context: Main launcher root search, no source filters, Notes enabled, query eligible. Expected behavior: Matching Notes append as passive Notes section according to configured passive source order. Edge cases: Empty/short/newline/advanced/disabled queries suppress Notes; cold cache may require a later frame to show ordinary passive hits. Shortcut/gesture: Type notes: meeting or n: meeting Context: Root launcher search with explicit Notes source filter. Expected behavior: Query strips to meeting; Notes is the only allowed passive source; source caps are raised; direct search path is used. Edge cases: Disabled passive default is overridden by explicit source intent; other source rows must not bleed in. Shortcut/gesture: Type attached source query, e.g. n:meeting or notes:meeting Context: Root launcher source-filter parsing. Expected behavior: Attached text becomes stripped free text; Notes search runs for meeting. Edge cases: n:not must find Welcome to Notes through bounded LIKE fallback if FTS returns empty. Shortcut/gesture: Type source-only n: / notes: Context: Root launcher with explicit Notes source and empty stripped query. Expected behavior: Shows pinned and most recently updated active notes as browse rows. Edge cases: Verify bare n: without trailing space separately; tests explicitly pin n: . Shortcut/gesture: Press Enter on selected Note row Context: A SearchResult::Note is selected in root launcher. Expected behavior: Calls execute_root_note_open, then open_note_in_notes_window; Notes window opens/focuses, note selected, launcher hides/resets. Edge cases: Existing Notes window must not close; stale/deleted note yields HUD failure. Shortcut/gesture: Move selection to a Note row via launcher selection controls or click Context: Grouped root results include a Notes section. Expected behavior: Selected row exposes Open Note as primary action and stable key note/{id}. Edge cases: launcher_command_id remains None; row is not shortcut/alias bindable. Shortcut/gesture: Type : / source heads Context: Menu syntax discoverability. Expected behavior: Plain : can open discoverability picker; active source-filter heads such as n: should not open the power/main hint. Edge cases: Unknown heads, quoted heads, malformed tokens, processes: / p: remain non-source-filter input. Scenarios Scenario name: Ordinary eligible query appends Notes passively Start state: Launcher open; Notes enabled; active note title/content matches query; query length meets minQueryChars. Steps: Type meeting; let passive cache/frame path resolve. Expected result: Notes section appears after Files/Browser Tabs and before Clipboard History / later passive sections / fallbacks; row shows title, pinned/update/char metadata. Verification signal: getState / preflight results include role=RootPassive, source Notes, type Note, action Open Note, no content body; static: append_root_notes_section. Scenario name: Source-filter Notes query only Start state: Launcher open; active matching note exists. Steps: Type n: meeting. Expected result: computed_search_text = "meeting"; source_filters = ["Notes"]; only Notes-allowed rows/status are shown. Verification signal: main_window_preflight exposes computed_search_text, source_filters, filter_indicators; source-filter grouping suppresses disallowed sources. Scenario name: Attached Notes source query Start state: Launcher open; active note Welcome to Notes exists. Steps: Type n:not. Expected result: Free text is not; row for Welcome to Notes appears via LIKE fallback if FTS misses. Verification signal: tests/menu_syntax_source_filters.rs#source_filters_accept_attached_query_text; src/notes/storage.rs unit test_search_root_notes_meta_matches_title_substrings_when_fts_has_no_hit. Scenario name: Source-only Notes browse Start state: Launcher open; multiple active notes with pinned/recent ordering. Steps: Type n: . Expected result: Notes rows show pinned and most recently updated active notes; no note body text. Verification signal: State rows under Notes; storage query returns empty-query active metadata; source audit requires pinned/recent active metadata for n: . Scenario name: Ineligible ordinary query suppresses Notes Start state: Launcher open; Notes enabled; matching notes exist. Steps: Try empty query, too-short query, multiline query, disabled config, and advanced predicate query. Expected result: No Notes section for ordinary ineligible states. Verification signal: root_notes_query_is_eligible; grouping test root_notes_rows_do_not_append_for_empty_short_disabled_or_advanced_query. Scenario name: Active-only metadata search Start state: Matching active note and matching soft-deleted note exist. Steps: Search the token. Expected result: Only active note appears; body content is not present in row/result model. Verification signal: root_unified_notes_search_is_metadata_only_bounded_and_active_only; n.deleted_at IS NULL; RootNoteSearchHit lacks full content. Scenario name: Enter opens closed Notes window Start state: Launcher open; Notes window closed; Note row selected. Steps: Press Enter. Expected result: Floating Notes window opens; selected note is loaded; launcher hides/resets. Verification signal: State-first proof: Notes host open, selected note id/title/editor content corresponds to row; main launcher hidden. Scenario name: Enter focuses existing Notes window Start state: Floating Notes window already open; launcher has selected root Note row. Steps: Press Enter on root Note row. Expected result: Existing Notes window remains open/focused and switches/selects note; it is not toggled closed. Verification signal: Before/after window handle/open-state unchanged except focus/selection; static audit proves open_notes_window absent from execute_root_note_open. Scenario name: Stale Note open failure Start state: Root Note row exists from prior results; note is deleted before Enter. Steps: Press Enter. Expected result: HUD says Failed to open note; launcher does not hide/reset on failure. Verification signal: State/HUD receipt; open_note_in_notes_window rejects missing/deleted note. Scenario name: Passive cache/source-filter isolation Start state: Same free text can match Notes and Clipboard/Files. Steps: Search n: plan, then clipboard: plan, then unfiltered plan. Expected result: Notes hits never bleed into non-Notes source-filter frames or unfiltered frames. Verification signal: RootPassiveFrameKey.source_filters; root_unified_source_filters_contract. Scenario name: Config clamping and parity Start state: User config changes Notes root search limits. Steps: Configure Notes values outside allowed ranges. Expected result: Runtime options clamp maxResults and minQueryChars; schema/defaults stay in sync. Verification signal: root_unified_config_schema_parity_contract; UnifiedSearchConfig::notes_section_options. Visual States State: Ordinary root results with Notes section What is visible: Section header Notes; one or more Note rows; row title or Untitled Note; subtitle Pinned · Updated <relative> · <n> chars when pinned. Focus owner: Main launcher search/list; selected row if navigated. Footer/actions/chrome: Primary action Open Note; type/source tag Note / Notes. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: HUD text/state receipt. State: No eligible Notes rows What is visible: No Notes section in ordinary root; fallback/other sections may remain. Under explicit source filter, filtered no-results/status surface may be visible. Focus owner: Launcher. Footer/actions/chrome: Shared empty/filter chrome. <!-- Source: Oracle session root-clipboard-feature-map, captured 2026-05-15. -->


008 Root Unified Search Clipboard History / Clipboard root rows / paste path Boundaries Owns: Root unified search Clipboard History rows in the main launcher ScriptList, represented as SearchResult::ClipboardHistory(ClipboardHistoryMatch). Passive, metadata-only clipboard matching for root queries via src/clipboard_history/database.rs#search_root_clipboard_history_meta, src/clipboard_history/cache.rs#search_root_clipboard_history_meta_cached, and src/clipboard_history/types.rs#RootClipboardHistorySectionOptions. Config path for ordinary passive visibility: unifiedSearch.clipboardHistory + global unifiedSearch.enabled + builtIns.clipboardHistory; default disabled. Explicit source heads clipboard: and c: as root source filters that opt Clipboard History into the current query/browse frame. Root row projection: title from metadata preview, subtitle from pinned/type/time metadata, type label Clipboard, source name Clipboard History, role rootPassive, stable key clipboard-history/{id}. Enter/paste path for root clipboard rows: execute_root_clipboard_history_paste → copy_entry_to_clipboard(entry_id) → hide_main_and_reset(cx) → delayed selected_text::simulate_paste_with_cg(). Source/static contracts listed in tests/source_audits/root_unified_clipboard_history_contract.rs and menu syntax cases in tests/menu_syntax_source_filters.rs. root-clipboard-feature-map Does not own: The full Clipboard History built-in surface in src/render_builtins/clipboard.rs: pagination, full history browsing, image previews, OCR rendering, pin/delete UI, Quick Look UI, sequential paste. Clipboard capture/retention/dedupe internals except where root search must consume bounded metadata only. Generic main-list selection, scrolling, fallback sections, source-filter parser ownership, or action-dialog infrastructure. Alias/shortcut binding for clipboard rows; launcher_command_id() is intentionally None. Raw clipboard content display in root search. Raw content may be loaded only on activation/action paths that already own clipboard copy/attach behavior. Adjacent feature dependencies: main-menu-search-selection: root filter text, grouped results, stable selection restoration, passive/fallback insertion. builtin-filterable-surfaces: existing clipboard history built-in and copy/paste behavior. storage-cache-security: SQLite metadata table, metadata cache, cache warmers, raw-content boundary. protocol-automation: mainWindowPreflight, getState, getElements, source filter receipts, visible row receipts. agentic-testing: state-first runtime proofs; screenshots/native input only for actual OS paste/focus behavior. theme-config-preferences: Rust config/schema/default parity for unifiedSearch.clipboardHistory. root_unified_result_actions: adjacent action-popup subject/action IDs; Feature 008 primarily owns Enter/root_clipboard_paste. User Stories As a user, I can enable root Clipboard History search and type a non-empty launcher query to see recent matching clipboard metadata alongside other passive sources. As a user, I can type c: skip, c:skip, or clipboard:skip to search only Clipboard History for skip, even when ordinary passive clipboard rows are disabled by default. As a user, I can type c: or clipboard: with no stripped search text to browse bounded recent clipboard metadata without enabling ordinary empty-root clipboard recents. As a user, I can recognize root clipboard rows by the Clipboard History section/source and Clipboard type label. As a user, I can press Enter on a root clipboard row and have that item copied back to the system clipboard, the launcher hidden, and Cmd+V simulated into the previously focused app. As a user, I should not see images/OCR/raw clipboard content surfaced by root Clipboard History search. As a user, I should not have primary commands, Files, Notes, or fallbacks mixed into a clipboard-only source-filter result unless I explicitly include another source filter too. As a reviewer, I can prove this feature without screenshots unless I need to prove actual native paste into another app. State Model Window/surface modes: Main launcher ScriptList root search mode. Ordinary passive root mode: clipboard rows may appear for eligible non-empty queries only when configured on. Source-filter mode: clipboard:/c: makes Clipboard History the selected root source for the stripped query. Source-filter browse mode: c: / clipboard: returns bounded recent metadata rows with empty stripped text. Advanced predicate mode: passive Clipboard History rows are suppressed when an advanced predicate query is active. Full Clipboard History built-in surface is separate and not owned here. Persistent data/storage: Clipboard DB metadata used for root rows: id, content_type, timestamp, pinned, text_preview, image_width, image_height, byte_size, ocr_text. Root search must use metadata only: get_clipboard_history_meta(options.scan_limit, 0) and entry.text_preview; no get_entry_content() during grouping/search. Eligible root content types: Text, Link, File, Color; Image excluded. Config/state: UnifiedSearchClipboardHistoryConfig, RootClipboardHistorySectionOptions, DEFAULT_UNIFIED_SEARCH_CLIPBOARD_HISTORY_ENABLED = false, schema field clipboardHistory?: UnifiedSearchClipboardHistoryConfig. Activation uses existing copy_entry_to_clipboard, so it inherits that helper’s existing DB/cache/clipboard side effects. Runtime caches/handles: RootPassiveFrameKey includes query, advanced-query flag, source filters, and clipboard options; identical frame key reuses frozen hits. RootPassiveFrame.clipboard_history_hits: Vec<ClipboardEntryMeta>. Ordinary passive search uses search_root_clipboard_history_meta_cached; cold cache returns no hits and starts a background refresh for future frames. Explicit c:/clipboard: uses search_root_clipboard_history_meta_direct and forces clipboard_history_options.enabled = true, min_query_chars = 0, and max-results cap raised to explicit-source target. Grouping uses append_root_clipboard_history_section and append_root_passive_section(..., "Clipboard History", ...). Result identity: history_result_key / stable selection key clipboard-history/{id}; launcher_command_id() == None; no generic frecency record on Enter. Preflight receipts expose content-light fields: role, type label, source name, stable key, source filters, visible row fingerprints, action kind. Error/empty/loading states: Default config: no ordinary passive clipboard rows. Empty ordinary root query: no clipboard rows. Short ordinary query below min_query_chars: no clipboard rows. Newline-containing query: ineligible. c: source-only browse: eligible because explicit source sets min_query_chars = 0. Cold ordinary passive cache: returns empty for current frame and warms cache; must not repaint current visible rows when warm completes. Explicit source no hits: source-filter status/no-results state, not fallback pollution. Paste copy failure: should not simulate paste; current audit pins the success path, not full failure UX. Simulated paste failure: logged after hide/copy path; native paste success is OS/focus dependent. Keystrokes And Commands Shortcut/gesture: Type ordinary root query, e.g. skip. Context: Main launcher root input, no active source filter, no advanced predicate. Expected behavior: If ordinary clipboard source is enabled and query is eligible, matching recent clipboard metadata appears under Clipboard History according to passive source order/budget. Edge cases: Disabled config, empty query, short query, newline query, advanced predicates, cold cache, or image-only matches produce no rows. Shortcut/gesture: Type c: skip, c:skip, clipboard: skip, or clipboard:skip. Context: Main launcher root input with Clipboard History source head. Expected behavior: Parser strips the source head, computes free text skip, enables Clipboard History for this frame, searches direct local metadata, and suppresses other root sources unless separately included. Edge cases: Quoted heads stay literal; unknown heads stay literal; source heads must be standalone/capture-safe. Multiple source heads are additive. Exclusion wins: including and excluding the same source should suppress it. Shortcut/gesture: Type c: or clipboard: . Context: Source-filter-only root input. Expected behavior: Browse bounded recent clipboard metadata from the metadata table/cache path without enabling ordinary empty-root clipboard rows. Edge cases: Still excludes images/OCR/raw content. Should show source-filter status/no-results chrome if nothing is available. Shortcut/gesture: Press Enter on selected Clipboard History root row. Context: Selected main-list item is SearchResult::ClipboardHistory. Expected behavior: Route to execute_root_clipboard_history_paste(&entry.id, cx). Copy selected entry through crate::clipboard_history::copy_entry_to_clipboard(entry_id). Hide/reset main window with hide_main_and_reset(cx). Spawn delayed paste simulation: sleep 100 ms, then crate::selected_text::simulate_paste_with_cg(). Edge cases: Missing DB entry/copy error should not paste stale clipboard content. Simulated paste can fail if macOS focus/permissions reject CG events; source audit can prove routing, native proof is needed for actual paste insertion. Shortcut/gesture: Open actions on selected root clipboard row. Context: Generic MainList root unified actions dialog. Expected behavior: At minimum, root_clipboard_paste must delegate to the same paste helper as Enter. Edge cases: Current action-contract excerpts also list copy/attach/pin/quick-look/delete; ownership is adjacent and should be reconciled with the lat first-pass note that root Clipboard rows exclude pin/delete/attach-to-AI. Shortcut/gesture: Type :. Context: Menu syntax discoverability. Expected behavior: Colon can open source-head discoverability. Edge cases: Completed source heads like c: / clipboard: should not open the unrelated power/hint popup. Scenarios Scenario name: Ordinary passive clipboard disabled by default.
