Open Questions / Gaps Gap: Lat says first-pass root Clipboard History excludes pin/delete and attach-to-AI actions, but root_unified_result_actions.rs / action matrix excerpts include root_clipboard_attach_to_ai, pin/unpin, Quick Look, and delete. Why it matters: Review agents need a single ownership boundary: Feature 008 primary Enter/paste only, or broader root clipboard actions too. Suggested next check: Reconcile lat.md/builtins#Root Unified Search Clipboard History with tests/source_audits/root_unified_source_actions_contract.rs and scripts/agentic/root-source-actions-matrix.ts. Gap: Paste failure UX is not fully pinned in the excerpt. Why it matters: If copy_entry_to_clipboard fails, the app must not hide and paste stale clipboard contents. Suggested next check: Inspect full execute_root_clipboard_history_paste error branch and add/source-audit HUD/log behavior if missing. Gap: Explicit c: appears to force clipboard_history_options.enabled = true, potentially bypassing both ordinary passive default and built-in gate. Why it matters: This is probably intentional explicit user selection, but privacy/config semantics should be documented clearly. Suggested next check: Confirm desired relationship among unifiedSearch.enabled, builtIns.clipboardHistory, and explicit source heads. Gap: Grouping maps ContentType::Image => "Image" if an image entry reaches append_root_clipboard_history_section, while producer eligibility excludes images. Why it matters: Producer-side exclusion is pinned, but a future caller could pass image metadata and make image rows visible. Suggested next check: Consider whether grouping should defensively filter root_clipboard_entry_is_eligible too. Gap: Native paste proof is inherently OS/focus dependent. Why it matters: Source/static and protocol proofs can pass while actual CG paste fails due to permissions or focus timing. Suggested next check: Keep native proof targeted and separate from routine regression checks; only run it for paste/focus regressions. 008 Root Unified Search Clipboard History / Clipboard root rows / paste path Boundaries Owns: Root unified search Clipboard History rows in the main launcher ScriptList, represented as SearchResult::ClipboardHistory(ClipboardHistoryMatch). Passive, metadata-only clipboard matching for root queries via src/clipboard_history/database.rs#search_root_clipboard_history_meta, src/clipboard_history/cache.rs#search_root_clipboard_history_meta_cached, and src/clipboard_history/types.rs#RootClipboardHistorySectionOptions. Config path for ordinary passive visibility: unifiedSearch.clipboardHistory + global unifiedSearch.enabled + builtIns.clipboardHistory; default disabled. Explicit source heads clipboard: and c: as root source filters that opt Clipboard History into the current query/browse frame. Root row projection: title from metadata preview, subtitle from pinned/type/time metadata, type label Clipboard, source name Clipboard History, role rootPassive, stable key clipboard-history/{id}. Enter/paste path for root clipboard rows: execute_root_clipboard_history_paste → copy_entry_to_clipboard(entry_id) → hide_main_and_reset(cx) → delayed selected_text::simulate_paste_with_cg(). Source/static contracts listed in tests/source_audits/root_unified_clipboard_history_contract.rs and menu syntax cases in tests/menu_syntax_source_filters.rs. root-clipboard-feature-map Does not own: The full Clipboard History built-in surface in src/render_builtins/clipboard.rs: pagination, full history browsing, image previews, OCR rendering, pin/delete UI, Quick Look UI, sequential paste. Clipboard capture/retention/dedupe internals except where root search must consume bounded metadata only. Generic main-list selection, scrolling, fallback sections, source-filter parser ownership, or action-dialog infrastructure. Alias/shortcut binding for clipboard rows; launcher_command_id() is intentionally None. Raw clipboard content display in root search. Raw content may be loaded only on activation/action paths that already own clipboard copy/attach behavior. Open Questions / Gaps Gap: Lat says first-pass root Clipboard History excludes pin/delete and attach-to-AI actions, but root_unified_result_actions.rs / action matrix excerpts include root_clipboard_attach_to_ai, pin/unpin, Quick Look, and delete. Why it matters: Review agents need a single ownership boundary: Feature 008 primary Enter/paste only, or broader root clipboard actions too. Gap: Paste failure UX is not fully pinned in the excerpt. Why it matters: If copy_entry_to_clipboard fails, the app must not hide and paste stale clipboard contents. Gap: Explicit c: appears to force clipboard_history_options.enabled = true, potentially bypassing both ordinary passive default and built-in gate. Why it matters: This is probably intentional explicit user selection, but privacy/config semantics should be documented clearly. Suggested next check: Confirm desired relationship among unifiedSearch.enabled, builtIns.clipboardHistory, and explicit source heads. Gap: Grouping maps ContentType::Image => "Image" if an image entry reaches append_root_clipboard_history_section, while producer eligibility excludes images. Why it matters: Producer-side exclusion is pinned, but a future caller could pass image metadata and make image rows visible. Suggested next check: Consider whether grouping should defensively filter root_clipboard_entry_is_eligible too. Gap: Native paste proof is inherently OS/focus dependent. Why it matters: Source/static and protocol proofs can pass while actual CG paste fails due to permissions or focus timing. Suggested next check: Keep native proof targeted and separate from routine regression checks; only run it for paste/focus regressions. Suggested next feature 009 Root Unified Search Dictation History / Dictation root rows / paste path


<!-- Source: Oracle session root-dictation-feature-map, captured 2026-05-15. -->


009 Root Unified Search Dictation History / Dictation root rows / paste path Boundaries Owns: opt-in passive Root Unified Search rows for saved Dictation History metadata, source-filter entry via dictation: / d:, row identity, selection behavior, and Enter-to-paste transcript loading. root-dictation-feature-map Owns: privacy/perf contract that root rows carry metadata only: id, preview, target, timestamp, audio_duration_ms, matched_field, subtitle, score; no full transcript until explicit Enter/action. Owns: local-only root search over compacted dictation-history.jsonl, bounded by scanLimit, default-disabled via unifiedSearch.dictationHistory. Does not own: microphone capture, transcription, waveform/UI overlay, dictation device setup, or how transcripts are originally recorded. Does not own: full Dictation History built-in surface in src/render_builtins/dictation_history.rs, except shared storage/search functions. Does not own: generic main launcher selection mechanics, generic passive source budgeting, generic source-filter parser infrastructure, generic actions-dialog hosting, or OS/native paste implementation. Adjacent feature dependencies: main-menu-search-selection for root result grouping/selection; builtin-filterable-surfaces for built-in Dictation History surface; dictation-media for saved transcripts and resources; storage-cache-security for JSONL/cache/privacy boundaries; protocol-automation / agentic-testing for state-first verification; root unified source filters and passive-frame stability contracts. User Stories As a user, I can opt into showing saved dictation transcripts as passive launcher results in Root Unified Search. As a user, I can type a normal query and see matching saved dictation metadata mixed into passive root sections when enabled. As a user, I can type dictation: standup or d: standup to search only saved dictation records. As a user, I can type dictation: or d: with no search text to browse recent saved dictation metadata. As a user, I can select a Dictation History row and press Enter to paste the full transcript into the target context. As a privacy-conscious user, I should not see or leak the full transcript in root result rows, state receipts, stable keys, launcher command IDs, or logs before explicit selection. As a reviewer, I can prove root Dictation History is opt-in, bounded, metadata-only, local-only, passive, and ordered/capped with the other passive sources. State Model Window/surface modes: Root launcher / ScriptList search mode; Dictation History rows appear as passive root results under the Dictation History section, not as the dedicated Dictation History built-in surface. Window/surface modes: source-filter mode when dictation: / d: is parsed; disallowed sources and primary handoff rows are suppressed according to root source-filter rules. Window/surface modes: predicated/advanced query mode suppresses Dictation History rows; source-filter-only syntax is allowed and can browse recent metadata. Persistent data/storage: saved local dictation-history.jsonl under Kit path via src/dictation/history.rs#history_path. Persistent data/storage: DictationHistoryEntry contains full transcript, preview, target, timestamp, duration, and id; root rows project only metadata. Persistent data/storage: unifiedSearch.dictationHistory config is default-disabled; defaults pinned as enabled false, maxResults = 3, minQueryChars = 4, scanLimit = 200. Persistent data/storage: normalized options clamp max_results to 1..=5, min_query_chars to 4..=32, and scan_limit to 25..=200 in UnifiedSearchConfig::dictation_history_section_options. Runtime caches/handles: RootPassiveFrameKey includes query, advanced-query state, source filters, and Dictation History options; same key reuses frozen hits. Runtime caches/handles: RootPassiveFrame.dictation_history_hits carries Vec<RootDictationHistorySearchHit>. Runtime caches/handles: non-explicit passive search uses search_root_dictation_history_cached; cache miss spawns root-dictation-history-cache, returns no current-frame hits, and must not publish into the active frame. Runtime caches/handles: explicit d: / dictation: uses search_root_dictation_history_direct, enables the source, lowers min chars to 0, and raises result cap toward passive explicit-source target. Runtime caches/handles: load_history() uses an mtime/signature-backed index cache; writes/deletes invalidate the cache. Error/empty/loading states: disabled source returns no root rows. Error/empty/loading states: ordinary empty query, too-short query, newline query, disabled config, or predicated advanced query returns no root rows. Error/empty/loading states: source-only d: / dictation: with no free text returns recent saved metadata if history exists. Error/empty/loading states: empty history yields no rows; adjacent kit://dictation advertises unavailable/hidden when no history exists. Error/empty/loading states: cold passive cache miss warms silently for future frames; no screenshot-visible loading spinner is expected for this source. Error/empty/loading states: missing selected entry id on Enter logs Root dictation history entry not found and shows HUD Failed to paste dictation. Keystrokes And Commands Shortcut/gesture: type a normal root query, for example standup. Context: launcher ScriptList root search; unifiedSearch.dictationHistory.enabled = true; query length meets minQueryChars. Expected behavior: matching saved dictation metadata appears as passive Dictation History rows, capped by passive budget and source max. Edge cases: no rows if disabled, too short, newline, predicated advanced query, no saved history, cache cold on non-explicit first frame, or passive budget exhausted. Shortcut/gesture: type dictation: standup. Context: root source-filter syntax; canonical Dictation source head. Expected behavior: stripped free text is standup; source filters include Dictation; Dictation History source is enabled for this frame and searched directly. Edge cases: source-filter token must be standalone/recognized; exclusion wins if source is excluded by structured filter syntax. Shortcut/gesture: type d:standup or d: standup. Context: short Dictation source head with attached or spaced query text. Expected behavior: parser strips d: and searches Dictation History with free text standup. Edge cases: project:d or unknown heads must not parse as Dictation source filters. Shortcut/gesture: type dictation: or d: with empty stripped text. Context: explicit source-only Dictation filter. Expected behavior: recent saved dictation metadata rows are shown; full transcript remains unloaded. Edge cases: ordinary empty root query remains ineligible; only explicit source filter lowers min query chars to zero. Shortcut/gesture: Arrow keys / list navigation. Context: main launcher list with Dictation History rows visible. Expected behavior: selection can land on SearchResult::DictationHistory; stable selection key is dictation-history/{id}. Edge cases: selection must be preserved by stable key across passive-frame cache updates; row is non-bindable and should not create launcher alias/shortcut command IDs. Shortcut/gesture: Enter on a selected Dictation History row. Context: selected SearchResult::DictationHistory. Expected behavior: calls execute_root_dictation_history_paste(&id), loads full entry via crate::dictation::get_history_entry(entry_id), then uses TextInjector::new() and injector.paste_text(&transcript). Edge cases: if entry was deleted/stale, show HUD failure; no transcript should have been loaded before this point. Shortcut/gesture: open root actions dialog on selected Dictation History row; exact binding is owned by generic actions-popup routing, not pinned in this bundle. Context: selected root Dictation row. Expected behavior: action subject stores only { id, preview }; actions include root_dictation_paste, root_dictation_copy_transcript, root_dictation_attach_to_ai, root_dictation_create_note, root_dictation_delete. Edge cases: transcript-loading actions must load by id only after explicit action; actionsDialog receipt must not expose transcript. Scenarios Scenario name: default privacy-off root search. Start state: saved dictation history exists; unifiedSearch.dictationHistory.enabled = false. Steps: open root launcher; type a matching query. Expected result: no Dictation History root rows. Verification signal: source audit sees default false; runtime mainWindowPreflight.visibleResults has no sourceName = "Dictation History". Scenario name: opt-in passive metadata result. Verification signal: tests/menu_syntax_source_filters.rs cases plus preflight filter indicators/source filters. Scenario name: ordinary ineligible query is suppressed. Start state: config enabled; saved entries exist. Steps: type empty ordinary query, a query shorter than min chars, or a query containing newline. Expected result: no Dictation History rows. Scenario name: stale row id on Enter. Start state: row selected from previous metadata; backing entry deleted before action. Steps: press Enter. Verification signal: source path in selection_fallback.rs; runtime can delete synthetic entry before Enter and assert HUD/state/log. Scenario name: passive cache cold start. Start state: non-explicit normal root query; JSONL exists but root dictation cache is cold. Steps: type matching query. Expected result: current frame returns no dictation hits, warms cache in background, and does not mutate active visible frame. Verification signal: passive snapshot audit sees search_root_dictation_history_cached, root-dictation-history-cache, and absence of invalidate_grouped_cache, publish_active_results, cx.notify. Scenario name: explicit source filter bypasses passive preview cap. Start state: many saved dictation entries; passive limits lower than explicit-source target. Steps: type d: or d: common. Expected result: explicit Dictation source raises max_results toward root_passive_result_limits.max_total_results; status row reflects shown/loaded. Verification signal: filtering_cache.rs explicit Dictation block sets enabled = true, min_query_chars = 0, and maxes result cap. Scenario name: root actions stay content-light. Start state: Dictation History row selected. Steps: open actions dialog. Expected result: actions list includes Paste, Copy Transcript, Attach to AI, Create Note from Transcript, Delete; stored subject is id+preview only. Verification signal: root_unified_source_actions_contract, scripts/agentic/root-source-actions-matrix.ts, and actionsDialog receipt absence of transcript. Answer:

009 Root Unified Search Dictation History / Dictation root rows / paste path Boundaries Owns: opt-in passive Root Unified Search rows for saved Dictation History metadata, source-filter entry via dictation: / d:, row identity, selection behavior, and Enter-to-paste transcript loading. root-dictation-feature-map Owns: privacy/perf contract that root rows carry metadata only: id, preview, target, timestamp, audio_duration_ms, matched_field, subtitle, score; no full transcript until explicit Enter/action. Owns: local-only root search over compacted dictation-history.jsonl, bounded by scanLimit, default-disabled via unifiedSearch.dictationHistory. Does not own: microphone capture, transcription, waveform/UI overlay, dictation device setup, or how transcripts are originally recorded. Does not own: full Dictation History built-in surface in src/render_builtins/dictation_history.rs, except shared storage/search functions. Does not own: generic main launcher selection mechanics, generic passive source budgeting, generic source-filter parser infrastructure, generic actions-dialog hosting, or OS/native paste implementation. Adjacent feature dependencies: main-menu-search-selection for root result grouping/selection; builtin-filterable-surfaces for built-in Dictation History surface; dictation-media for saved transcripts and resources; storage-cache-security for JSONL/cache/privacy boundaries; protocol-automation / agentic-testing for state-first verification; root unified source filters and passive-frame stability contracts. User Stories As a user, I can opt into showing saved dictation transcripts as passive launcher results in Root Unified Search. As a user, I can type a normal query and see matching saved dictation metadata mixed into passive root sections when enabled. As a user, I can type dictation: standup or d: standup to search only saved dictation records. As a user, I can type dictation: or d: with no search text to browse recent saved dictation metadata. As a user, I can select a Dictation History row and press Enter to paste the full transcript into the target context. As a privacy-conscious user, I should not see or leak the full transcript in root result rows, state receipts, stable keys, launcher command IDs, or logs before explicit selection. As a reviewer, I can prove root Dictation History is opt-in, bounded, metadata-only, local-only, passive, and ordered/capped with the other passive sources. State Model Window/surface modes: Root launcher / ScriptList search mode; Dictation History rows appear as passive root results under the Dictation History section, not as the dedicated Dictation History built-in surface. Window/surface modes: source-filter mode when dictation: / d: is parsed; disallowed sources and primary handoff rows are suppressed according to root source-filter rules. Window/surface modes: predicated/advanced query mode suppresses Dictation History rows; source-filter-only syntax is allowed and can browse recent metadata. Persistent data/storage: saved local dictation-history.jsonl under Kit path via src/dictation/history.rs#history_path. Persistent data/storage: DictationHistoryEntry contains full transcript, preview, target, timestamp, duration, and id; root rows project only metadata. Persistent data/storage: unifiedSearch.dictationHistory config is default-disabled; defaults pinned as enabled false, maxResults = 3, minQueryChars = 4, scanLimit = 200. Persistent data/storage: normalized options clamp max_results to 1..=5, min_query_chars to 4..=32, and scan_limit to 25..=200 in UnifiedSearchConfig::dictation_history_section_options. Runtime caches/handles: RootPassiveFrameKey includes query, advanced-query state, source filters, and Dictation History options; same key reuses frozen hits. Runtime caches/handles: RootPassiveFrame.dictation_history_hits carries Vec<RootDictationHistorySearchHit>. Runtime caches/handles: non-explicit passive search uses search_root_dictation_history_cached; cache miss spawns root-dictation-history-cache, returns no current-frame hits, and must not publish into the active frame. Runtime caches/handles: explicit d: / dictation: uses search_root_dictation_history_direct, enables the source, lowers min chars to 0, and raises result cap toward passive explicit-source target. Runtime caches/handles: load_history() uses an mtime/signature-backed index cache; writes/deletes invalidate the cache. Error/empty/loading states: disabled source returns no root rows. Error/empty/loading states: ordinary empty query, too-short query, newline query, disabled config, or predicated advanced query returns no root rows. Error/empty/loading states: source-only d: / dictation: with no free text returns recent saved metadata if history exists. Error/empty/loading states: empty history yields no rows; adjacent kit://dictation advertises unavailable/hidden when no history exists. Error/empty/loading states: cold passive cache miss warms silently for future frames; no screenshot-visible loading spinner is expected for this source. Error/empty/loading states: missing selected entry id on Enter logs Root dictation history entry not found and shows HUD Failed to paste dictation. Keystrokes And Commands Shortcut/gesture: type a normal root query, for example standup. Context: launcher ScriptList root search; unifiedSearch.dictationHistory.enabled = true; query length meets minQueryChars. Expected behavior: matching saved dictation metadata appears as passive Dictation History rows, capped by passive budget and source max. Edge cases: no rows if disabled, too short, newline, predicated advanced query, no saved history, cache cold on non-explicit first frame, or passive budget exhausted. Shortcut/gesture: type dictation: standup. Context: root source-filter syntax; canonical Dictation source head. Expected behavior: stripped free text is standup; source filters include Dictation; Dictation History source is enabled for this frame and searched directly. Edge cases: source-filter token must be standalone/recognized; exclusion wins if source is excluded by structured filter syntax. Shortcut/gesture: type d:standup or d: standup. Context: short Dictation source head with attached or spaced query text. Expected behavior: parser strips d: and searches Dictation History with free text standup. Edge cases: project:d or unknown heads must not parse as Dictation source filters. Shortcut/gesture: type dictation: or d: with empty stripped text. Context: explicit source-only Dictation filter. Expected behavior: recent saved dictation metadata rows are shown; full transcript remains unloaded. Edge cases: ordinary empty root query remains ineligible; only explicit source filter lowers min query chars to zero. Shortcut/gesture: Arrow keys / list navigation. Context: main launcher list with Dictation History rows visible. Expected behavior: selection can land on SearchResult::DictationHistory; stable selection key is dictation-history/{id}. Edge cases: selection must be preserved by stable key across passive-frame cache updates; row is non-bindable and should not create launcher alias/shortcut command IDs. Shortcut/gesture: Enter on a selected Dictation History row. Context: selected SearchResult::DictationHistory. Expected behavior: calls execute_root_dictation_history_paste(&id), loads full entry via crate::dictation::get_history_entry(entry_id), then uses TextInjector::new() and injector.paste_text(&transcript). Edge cases: if entry was deleted/stale, show HUD failure; no transcript should have been loaded before this point. Shortcut/gesture: open root actions dialog on selected Dictation History row; exact binding is owned by generic actions-popup routing, not pinned in this bundle. Context: selected root Dictation row. Expected behavior: action subject stores only { id, preview }; actions include root_dictation_paste, root_dictation_copy_transcript, root_dictation_attach_to_ai, root_dictation_create_note, root_dictation_delete. Edge cases: transcript-loading actions must load by id only after explicit action; actionsDialog receipt must not expose transcript. Scenarios Scenario name: default privacy-off root search. Verification Map Source/static checks: cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_dictation_history_contract -- --nocapture. Source/static checks: cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_source_filters_contract -- --nocapture for dictation: / d: parsing, source gating, explicit-source cap raise, and no hint popup. Source/static checks: cargo test --test menu_syntax_source_filters -- --nocapture for canonical, short, attached, spaced, and source-only filter cases. Source/static checks: cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_config_schema_parity_contract -- --nocapture for config/schema/default/options parity and passive source ordering. Source/static checks: cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_passive_snapshot_contract -- --nocapture for cache-only foreground search, background warmer, passive score cap, and mtime-backed JSONL index. Source/static checks: cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_search_stability_contract -- --nocapture for rootPassive role, stable selection key receipts, visible-result fingerprints, and state-first proof scaffolding. Source/static checks: cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_source_actions_contract -- --nocapture for root action ids, id+preview-only subject, and no transcript in action receipts. Source/static checks: cargo check --lib, cargo fmt --check, git diff --check, lat check. Runtime/state-first proofs: create a synthetic saved dictation entry in the test Kit path; enable unifiedSearch.dictationHistory; use setFilter and mainWindowPreflight to prove role/source/type/stable key/action label without screenshots. Runtime/state-first proofs: filter d: and assert computed_search_text = "", source_filters contains dictation, recent metadata rows appear, and no transcript appears in receipts. Runtime/state-first proofs: filter d: unique-token and assert the selected row stable key is dictation-history/{synthetic-id} with enterAction present. Runtime/state-first proofs: verify disabled config and ordinary short/empty/newline/predicated query states produce no Dictation History rows. Runtime/state-first proofs: verify cold non-explicit cache does not change visibleResultKeyFingerprint / visibleRowFingerprint while the background warmer runs. Runtime/state-first proofs: action dialog proof should inspect visibleActions ids/labels and confirm absence of transcript, rawClipboard, or note body-style content. Visual/native proofs only if needed: screenshot only if row layout, section header, status/chip rendering, or empty-filter text is disputed and state receipts cannot prove it. Visual/native proofs only if needed: native paste proof only if validating actual OS paste delivery into an external app; otherwise source audit plus controlled state/action receipts are the right proof tier. Open Questions / Gaps Gap: exact keyboard shortcut for opening the actions dialog is not present in the provided bundle. Why it matters: this map can pin action behavior but not the physical shortcut. Suggested next check: inspect actions-popups, keyboard-focus-routing, or action-toggle keybinding docs/tests. Gap: SourceHeadSpec for Dictation shows planned: true in src/menu_syntax/payload.rs while root Dictation History behavior is implemented. Why it matters: discoverability UI may label an implemented source as planned, depending on how planned is rendered. Suggested next check: inspect source-head picker rendering and decide whether this flag is stale or intentionally means “source-filter planned metadata.” Gap: runtime cache-warm status for Dictation History is less observable than browser passive snapshot sources. Why it matters: state-first proof of cold-cache warmup may need a two-frame query or synthetic prewarm rather than waiting on a refreshing receipt. Suggested next check: run or inspect the passive-frame stability proof with synthetic dictation history and decide whether a content-free dictation cache status receipt is warranted. Gap: ownership of non-paste dictation root actions is adjacent. Why it matters: Copy Transcript, Attach to AI, Create Note, and Delete also load transcript or mutate history after explicit action; they share the privacy invariant but are broader than the Enter paste path. Suggested next check: map those under a root unified source-actions feature or Dictation History actions feature. Suggested next feature 010 Root Unified Search ACP History / AI Conversations root rows / resume path


<!-- Source: Oracle session root-acp-history-feature-map, captured 2026-05-15. -->


010 Root Unified Search ACP History / AI Conversations root rows / resume path Boundaries Owns: Root launcher passive AI Conversations rows backed by saved ACP conversation history. SearchResult::AcpHistory(AcpHistoryMatch) launcher metadata: title, subtitle, type label AI Conversation, source AI Conversations, default action Resume Conversation, stable key acp-history/{session_id}, and non-bindable command identity. unifiedSearch.acpHistory config surface: enabled, maxResults, minQueryChars, clamped through UnifiedSearchConfig::acp_history_section_options. Source-filter integration for conversations: / ai: as RootUnifiedSourceFilter::Conversations. Passive root grouping through append_root_acp_history_section, using append_root_passive_section. Selection/Enter wiring from root row to ScriptListApp::resume_acp_conversation_from_history. Root-row action subject/action coverage for ACP History: resume, copy title, copy session id, copy preview. Does not own: ACP chat lifecycle internals, streaming, cancellation, model/agent selection, detached-window policy beyond calling the shared resume helper. ACP composer context staging, attachment tokens, slash/mention picker, or attach-summary actions. Root search explicitly does not expose attach-summary for ACP History in this pass. ACP History built-in browser UI behavior such as its list preview, delete shortcut, or empty strings, except that it shares the resume helper. General source-filter parser design, except that Conversations aliases must keep working. Root file search provider behavior, except the invariant that ACP rows must not split the Files section or Search Files continuation row. Full storage lifecycle for saved conversations, except root-search read/cache expectations and history-cache invalidation on writes/deletes. Adjacent feature dependencies: main-menu-search-selection: grouped root rows, selected row resolution, stable selection restoration. acp-chat-core: resume_acp_conversation_from_history, detached/embedded Agent Chat reuse, resume fallback. builtin-filterable-surfaces: ACP History built-in browser shares storage/search/resume concepts. storage-cache-security: acp-history.jsonl, acp-conversations/{session_id}.json, mtime-backed index cache, bounded search_text. protocol-automation + agentic-testing: state-first receipts via mainWindowPreflight, getState, waitFor, getElements, rootPassiveFrame. theme-config-preferences: config/schema parity for unifiedSearch.acpHistory. root_unified_source_actions: action popup coverage for RootUnifiedActionSubject::AcpHistory. User Stories As a user, I can type an eligible root query and see saved AI conversations appear under an AI Conversations section without those rows outranking commands, scripts, apps, skills, windows, actions, or root file rows. root-acp-history-feature-map As a user, I can type ai: plan or conversations: plan to search saved AI conversation records as an explicit source-filtered root search. As a user, I can type source-only ai: or conversations: to browse recent saved conversation metadata, while ordinary empty root search stays free of saved conversations. As a user, I can select an AI conversation row and press Enter to resume that saved ACP conversation through the same resume path used by the ACP History browser. As a user, I can recognize ACP History rows by title, preview/message-count subtitle, source AI Conversations, type label AI Conversation, and default action Resume Conversation. As a user, I can open actions for a focused ACP History root row and run Resume Conversation, Copy Conversation Title, Copy Session ID, or Copy Preview; there is no root attach-summary action in this feature. As a user, I should not see ACP History rows for short ordinary queries, disabled config, disallowed source filters, or predicate-style advanced queries. State Model Window/surface modes: Main launcher / ScriptList root unified search, ordinary query. Main launcher / ScriptList with RootUnifiedSourceFilter::Conversations active from ai: or conversations:. Source-only browse mode for ai: / conversations: with stripped search text empty. Root passive query frame: RootPassiveFrameKey includes query text, advanced-query state, source filters, and ACP history options; RootPassiveFrame carries acp_history_hits. ACP Chat after resume: embedded or detached Agent Chat, depending on existing ACP window state handled by shared ACP logic. Adjacent, not owned: AcpHistoryView built-in browser, which also calls resume_acp_conversation_from_history. Persistent data/storage: src/ai/acp/history.rs summary index: acp-history.jsonl. Full saved conversation payloads: acp-conversations/{session_id}.json. AcpHistoryEntry: timestamp, first_message, message_count, session_id, title, preview, search_text. Legacy entries are back-filled on read; search_text is normalized/bounded before ranking. Config: Rust UnifiedSearchAcpHistoryConfig, TypeScript schema acpHistory?: UnifiedSearchAcpHistoryConfig, defaults prefixed DEFAULT_UNIFIED_SEARCH_ACP_HISTORY_. Runtime caches/handles: ACP_HISTORY_INDEX_CACHE: mtime/size-signature-backed index cache. ACP_HISTORY_REFRESH_IN_FLIGHT: prevents duplicate background warmers. Ordinary root passive search uses search_history_cached; cold/stale cache warms future frames without publishing into the active frame. Explicit Conversations source filter can use search_history_direct and raises caps/min chars for browse. Stable row identity: acp-history/{session_id} for selection/history/action context. Non-bindable command identity: SearchResult::AcpHistory(_) => None for launcher_command_id. Action popup subject: RootUnifiedActionSubject::AcpHistory(AcpHistoryEntry). Automation receipts: visibleResults, selectedResultKey, visibleResultKeyFingerprint, sourceFilters, rootPassiveFrame. Error/empty/loading states: Ordinary empty root query: no ACP History rows. Ordinary query below minQueryChars: no ACP History rows. unifiedSearch.enabled = false or unifiedSearch.acpHistory.enabled = false: no ACP History rows. Predicate advanced query: no ACP History rows. Explicit ai: / conversations: with no stripped text: recent saved conversation metadata; if none, source-filter empty state/status should be visible. Cold/stale cache in ordinary passive mode: current frame may show no ACP rows; background cache warms future frames and must not notify/publish into the active root frame. Missing/deleted conversation JSON on resume: handled by shared resume helper; exact user-facing failure/fallback UX is not fully pinned by the root ACP History audit. Keystrokes And Commands Shortcut/gesture: Type ordinary root query text. Context: Main launcher / ScriptList root search. Expected behavior: If query is eligible and config allows it, append AI Conversations rows from saved ACP history after primary/root-file results and before fallback handoff rows. Edge cases: Empty root, short query, disabled config, predicate advanced query, or excluded Conversations source produce no rows. Shortcut/gesture: Type ai: <query> or conversations: <query>. Context: Main launcher source-filtered root search. Expected behavior: Strip the source head, search only allowed Conversations source rows, raise passive caps for explicit source filtering, and expose source-filter receipt state. Edge cases: Attached form ai:plan should parse; malformed/unknown heads should not parse as source filters; exclusion wins if Conversations is both included and excluded. Shortcut/gesture: Type source-only ai: or conversations:. Context: Main launcher source-only browse. Expected behavior: Browse recent saved conversation metadata for AI Conversations only; ordinary empty launcher remains unaffected. Edge cases: No saved conversations should report source-filter empty/no-results state, not fall back to ordinary empty root ACP rows. Shortcut/gesture: Up/Down. Context: Main launcher result list with ACP History rows. Expected behavior: Standard row selection moves across grouped rows; ACP History selection key remains acp-history/{session_id}. Edge cases: Late passive cache warm must not change the active frame selection/fingerprint. Shortcut/gesture: Enter. Context: Focused SearchResult::AcpHistory root row. Expected behavior: Calls resume_acp_conversation_from_history(&session_id, first_message, cx) and opens/resumes Agent Chat with saved messages. Edge cases: No launcher frecency/bindable alias should be recorded for the row; existing detached ACP window is reused by shared ACP logic. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+K / shared actions dialog. Context: Focused ACP History root row in MainList. Expected behavior: Captures RootUnifiedActionSubject::AcpHistory and shows stable root actions: root_acp_history_resume, root_acp_history_copy_title, root_acp_history_copy_session_id, root_acp_history_copy_preview. Edge cases: Known action IDs without a captured subject must no-op/return, not fall through to generic script action handling; no attach-summary action. Shortcut/gesture: Escape. Context: Actions popup or resumed ACP surface. Expected behavior: Popup close returns focus to launcher; ACP close/return behavior belongs to acp-chat-core. Edge cases: Root ACP History should not invent a separate return-origin contract. Scenarios Scenario name: Ordinary root query shows AI Conversations passively. Start state: Main launcher open; unifiedSearch.acpHistory.enabled = true; saved ACP history cache warm; query length >= min chars. Steps: Type design. Expected result: Primary/root-file rows stay above passive rows; AI Conversations section appears with matching saved conversations; fallback handoff rows remain below. Verification signal: mainWindowPreflight.visibleResults[*] includes role=rootPassive, typeLabel=AI Conversation, sourceName=AI Conversations, stableKey=acp-history/{session_id}; grouped header order shows no Files split. Scenario name: Explicit ai: source-filter search. Start state: Main launcher open; saved ACP history exists. Steps: Type ai: refactor. Expected result: Computed free text is refactor; sourceFilters=["conversations"]; ACP History rows are allowed/direct-searched; primary/disallowed sources are suppressed as expected for source filters. Verification signal: mainWindowPreflight.sourceFilters, visibleResults source names, and source status rows/chips; scripts/agentic/root-source-filter-matrix.ts equivalent proof. Scenario name: Source-only AI Conversations browse. Start state: Main launcher open; saved ACP history exists. Steps: Type ai: or conversations:. Expected result: Recent saved conversation metadata appears under AI Conversations; ordinary empty root query still shows no saved conversations. Verification signal: Parser returns source-filter-only advanced query with empty free text; visibleResults contains only conversation rows/status for source-filter browse. Scenario name: Enter resumes selected conversation. Start state: Main launcher showing an ACP History row with session_id=s1. Steps: Select row, press Enter. Expected result: selection_fallback.rs dispatches SearchResult::AcpHistory to resume_acp_conversation_from_history; ACP Chat resumes saved messages for s1. Verification signal: State-first ACP receipt shows Agent Chat active/resumed session; source audit verifies SearchResult::AcpHistory(acp_history_match) calls the shared helper. root-acp-history-feature-map Scenario name: Detached ACP reuse. Start state: Detached Agent Chat already open; launcher shows ACP History row. Steps: Select row, press Enter. Expected result: Shared resume helper updates/focuses detached ACP view instead of opening duplicate chat. Verification signal: ACP/window state shows one detached ACP surface and resumed target session; no duplicate ACP window. Scenario name: Cold passive cache does not mutate current frame. Start state: Main launcher open; ACP history cache cold/stale. Steps: Type eligible ordinary query. Expected result: Current frame may return zero ACP hits; background root-acp-history-cache warms cache; no cx.notify, no active frame publish, no grouped cache invalidation. Verification signal: rootPassiveFrame fingerprint/selection remains stable; later query/frame may show warmed hits. Scenario name: Short/predicate/disabled suppression. Start state: Main launcher open; saved ACP history exists. Steps: Type short ordinary query like ai, type predicate advanced query, or disable unifiedSearch.acpHistory. Expected result: No ACP History rows are appended. Verification signal: Unit/source tests around root_acp_history_query_is_eligible, append_root_acp_history_section, and disabled options. Scenario name: File-section regression guard. Start state: Main launcher has primary row, Files section, file rows, and Search Files continuation row. Steps: Type a query that also matches ACP history. Expected result: AI Conversations inserts after the complete Files section/continuation, not between file rows. Verification signal: root_acp_history_rows_do_not_split_files_section_or_file_handoff and root_unified_acp_history_contract. Scenario name: Root row actions. Start state: ACP History root row focused in MainList. Steps: Open actions dialog. Expected result: Resume/copy metadata actions are visible; selected action executes against captured AcpHistoryEntry. Verification signal: actionsDialog.visibleActions, contextStableKey=acp-history/{session_id}, and scripts/agentic/root-source-actions-matrix.ts expected actions. root-acp-history-feature-map Visual States State: Ordinary root search with AI Conversations hits. What is visible: Main launcher list; primary/root-file rows first; section header AI Conversations; rows titled from entry.title_display() with subtitle {preview_display()} · {message_count} message(s). Focus owner: Main launcher filter/list selection. Footer/actions/chrome: Standard main-list chrome; selected row default action text Resume Conversation; type/source metadata reports AI Conversation / AI Conversations. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: mainWindowPreflight.visibleResults[*].role=rootPassive, typeLabel, sourceName, stableKey, actionKind. State: ai: / conversations: source-filtered browse/search. What is visible: AI Conversations rows and source-filter status/chip rows; disallowed sources suppressed. Focus owner: Main launcher filter/list selection. Footer/actions/chrome: Source-filter no-results copy if empty; standard row actions if a row is selected. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: sourceFilters=["conversations"], filterIndicators, cached_source_statuses_snapshot. State: Focused ACP History root row. What is visible: Selected row highlight on conversation title; preview/message-count subtitle; action affordance reads Resume Conversation. Focus owner: Main list selected row while input remains launcher-owned. Footer/actions/chrome: Main-list footer/action hint; Cmd+K/shared action dialog available. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: selectedResultKey=acp-history/{session_id}, selectedResultRole=rootPassive. State: Root actions dialog for ACP History. What is visible: Actions for resume/copy title/copy session id/copy preview. Focus owner: Actions dialog. Footer/actions/chrome: Popup chrome; close restores MainList focus. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: actionsDialog.visibleActions, contextStableKey=acp-history/{session_id}. State: Resumed Agent Chat. What is visible: Agent Chat surface with saved conversation loaded, or fallback seeded from first message if shared resume cannot load the saved transcript. Focus owner: ACP Chat view/composer. Footer/actions/chrome: ACP-owned footer/actions, not root launcher footer. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: ACP state receipt / getAcpState session or message evidence. State: Adjacent ACP History browser empty/list. What is visible: acp-history-list, or No conversation history / No conversations match your filter. Focus owner: ACP History built-in view. Footer/actions/chrome: Built-in ACP History footer. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: ACP_HISTORY_POPUP_AUTOMATION_ID / built-in view receipts where available; not owned by root rows. Invariants And Regression Risks Invariant: ACP History root rows are passive launcher results, never primary/promoted results. Why it matters: Saved conversations must not steal intent from commands, scripts, apps, skills, windows, actions, or file rows. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/builtins#Root Unified Search ACP History; src/scripts/search/unified.rs; src/scripts/grouping.rs; tests/source_audits/root_unified_acp_history_contract.rs. Invariant: ACP rows insert after primary/root file rows and before fallback handoff rows. Why it matters: Preserves root launcher intent and fallback discoverability. Files/tests that pin it: append_root_acp_history_section; append_root_passive_section; root_acp_history_rows_insert_after_primary_rows_before_fallbacks. Invariant: ACP rows must not split the Files section or Search Files continuation row. Why it matters: Prevents the exact passive-source regression called out as critical in verification guidance. Files/tests that pin it: root_acp_history_rows_do_not_split_files_section_or_file_handoff; root_unified_acp_history_uses_passive_grouping_contract; verification guidance. root-acp-history-feature-map Invariant: ACP History rows are stable but non-bindable. Why it matters: Selection restoration/action context need stable identity, but saved conversations should not become shortcut aliases/launcher commands. Files/tests that pin it: AcpHistoryMatch; SearchResult::AcpHistory; history_result_key/stable_selection_key as acp-history/{session_id}; launcher_command_id => None; root_unified_acp_history_result_is_stable_and_non_bindable. Invariant: Enter path uses only the shared ACP history resume helper. Why it matters: Root search must not fork ACP resume semantics from the built-in history browser. Files/tests that pin it: src/app_impl/selection_fallback.rs; src/render_builtins/acp_history.rs#ScriptListApp#resume_acp_conversation_from_history; root_unified_acp_history_enter_resumes_existing_helper. Invariant: Ordinary passive root search is cache-only and frame-frozen. Why it matters: Prevents blocking JSONL reads, late-result UI churn, selection movement, and frame instability while typing. Files/tests that pin it: search_history_cached; root_passive_frame_for_current_query; root_unified_passive_snapshot_contract; root-passive-frame-stability.ts. Invariant: Explicit Conversations source filters can browse even with empty stripped text. Why it matters: Source-only ai: is a user-facing browse path, while ordinary empty root remains clean. Visual/native proofs only if needed: Screenshot only for row rendering/header order if state receipts cannot prove visual grouping. No screenshot is needed for cache stability, source-filter state, stable keys, or action IDs. Why it matters: Future agents may accidentally add attach-to-AI/summary actions under the ACP History root row. Why it matters: Reordering passive sources could accidentally violate the root file/fallback boundary. Suggested next check: Add a focused grouping test for custom order with ACP History still after Files and before fallback. Gap: Runtime resume proof is not named in the bundle the way source/filter/action matrix scripts are. Why it matters: Source audits prove wiring, but not the full user-visible resume result. Legacy entries are back-filled on read; search_text is normalized/bounded before ranking. Config: Rust UnifiedSearchAcpHistoryConfig, TypeScript schema acpHistory?: UnifiedSearchAcpHistoryConfig, defaults prefixed DEFAULT_UNIFIED_SEARCH_ACP_HISTORY_. Runtime caches/handles: ACP_HISTORY_INDEX_CACHE: mtime/size-signature-backed index cache. ACP_HISTORY_REFRESH_IN_FLIGHT: prevents duplicate background warmers. Ordinary root passive search uses search_history_cached; cold/stale cache warms future frames without publishing into the active frame. Explicit Conversations source filter can use search_history_direct and raises caps/min chars for browse. Stable row identity: acp-history/{session_id} for selection/history/action context. Non-bindable command identity: SearchResult::AcpHistory(_) => None for launcher_command_id. Action popup subject: RootUnifiedActionSubject::AcpHistory(AcpHistoryEntry). Automation receipts: visibleResults, selectedResultKey, visibleResultKeyFingerprint, sourceFilters, rootPassiveFrame. Error/empty/loading states: Ordinary empty root query: no ACP History rows. Ordinary query below minQueryChars: no ACP History rows. unifiedSearch.enabled = false or unifiedSearch.acpHistory.enabled = false: no ACP History rows. Predicate advanced query: no ACP History rows. Explicit ai: / conversations: with no stripped text: recent saved conversation metadata; if none, source-filter empty state/status should be visible. Cold/stale cache in ordinary passive mode: current frame may show no ACP rows; background cache warms future frames and must not notify/publish into the active root frame. Missing/deleted conversation JSON on resume: handled by shared resume helper; exact user-facing failure/fallback UX is not fully pinned by the root ACP History audit. Keystrokes And Commands Shortcut/gesture: Type ordinary root query text. Context: Main launcher / ScriptList root search. Expected behavior: If query is eligible and config allows it, append AI Conversations rows from saved ACP history after primary/root-file results and before fallback handoff rows. Edge cases: Empty root, short query, disabled config, predicate advanced query, or excluded Conversations source produce no rows. Shortcut/gesture: Type ai: <query> or conversations: <query>. Context: Main launcher source-filtered root search. Expected behavior: Strip the source head, search only allowed Conversations source rows, raise passive caps for explicit source filtering, and expose source-filter receipt state. Edge cases: Attached form ai:plan should parse; malformed/unknown heads should not parse as source filters; exclusion wins if Conversations is both included and excluded. Shortcut/gesture: Type source-only ai: or conversations:. Context: Main launcher source-only browse. Expected behavior: Browse recent saved conversation metadata for AI Conversations only; ordinary empty launcher remains unaffected. Edge cases: No saved conversations should report source-filter empty/no-results state, not fall back to ordinary empty root ACP rows. Shortcut/gesture: Up/Down. Context: Main launcher result list with ACP History rows. Expected behavior: Standard row selection moves across grouped rows; ACP History selection key remains acp-history/{session_id}. Edge cases: Late passive cache warm must not change the active frame selection/fingerprint. Shortcut/gesture: Enter. Context: Focused SearchResult::AcpHistory root row. Expected behavior: Calls resume_acp_conversation_from_history(&session_id, first_message, cx) and opens/resumes Agent Chat with saved messages. Edge cases: No launcher frecency/bindable alias should be recorded for the row; existing detached ACP window is reused by shared ACP logic. Shortcut/gesture: Cmd+K / shared actions dialog. Context: Focused ACP History root row in MainList. Expected behavior: Captures RootUnifiedActionSubject::AcpHistory and shows stable root actions: root_acp_history_resume, root_acp_history_copy_title, root_acp_history_copy_session_id, root_acp_history_copy_preview. Edge cases: Known action IDs without a captured subject must no-op/return, not fall through to generic script action handling; no attach-summary action. Shortcut/gesture: Escape. Context: Actions popup or resumed ACP surface. Expected behavior: Popup close returns focus to launcher; ACP close/return behavior belongs to acp-chat-core. Edge cases: Root ACP History should not invent a separate return-origin contract. Scenarios Scenario name: Ordinary root query shows AI Conversations passively. Start state: Main launcher open; unifiedSearch.acpHistory.enabled = true; saved ACP history cache warm; query length >= min chars. Steps: Type design. Expected result: Primary/root-file rows stay above passive rows; AI Conversations section appears with matching saved conversations; fallback handoff rows remain below. Verification signal: mainWindowPreflight.visibleResults[*] includes role=rootPassive, typeLabel=AI Conversation, sourceName=AI Conversations, stableKey=acp-history/{session_id}; grouped header order shows no Files split. Scenario name: Explicit ai: source-filter search. Start state: Main launcher open; saved ACP history exists. Steps: Type ai: refactor. Expected result: Computed free text is refactor; sourceFilters=["conversations"]; ACP History rows are allowed/direct-searched; primary/disallowed sources are suppressed as expected for source filters. Verification signal: mainWindowPreflight.sourceFilters, visibleResults source names, and source status rows/chips; scripts/agentic/root-source-filter-matrix.ts equivalent proof. Scenario name: Source-only AI Conversations browse. Start state: Main launcher open; saved ACP history exists. Steps: Type ai: or conversations:. Expected result: Recent saved conversation metadata appears under AI Conversations; ordinary empty root query still shows no saved conversations. Verification signal: Parser returns source-filter-only advanced query with empty free text; visibleResults contains only conversation rows/status for source-filter browse. Scenario name: Enter resumes selected conversation. Start state: Main launcher showing an ACP History row with session_id=s1. Steps: Select row, press Enter. Expected result: selection_fallback.rs dispatches SearchResult::AcpHistory to resume_acp_conversation_from_history; ACP Chat resumes saved messages for s1. Verification signal: State-first ACP receipt shows Agent Chat active/resumed session; source audit verifies SearchResult::AcpHistory(acp_history_match) calls the shared helper. root-acp-history-feature-map Scenario name: Detached ACP reuse. Start state: Detached Agent Chat already open; launcher shows ACP History row. Steps: Select row, press Enter. Expected result: Shared resume helper updates/focuses detached ACP view instead of opening duplicate chat. Verification signal: ACP/window state shows one detached ACP surface and resumed target session; no duplicate ACP window. Scenario name: Cold passive cache does not mutate current frame. Start state: Main launcher open; ACP history cache cold/stale. Steps: Type eligible ordinary query. Expected result: Current frame may return zero ACP hits; background root-acp-history-cache warms cache; no cx.notify, no active frame publish, no grouped cache invalidation. Verification signal: rootPassiveFrame fingerprint/selection remains stable; later query/frame may show warmed hits. Scenario name: Short/predicate/disabled suppression. Start state: Main launcher open; saved ACP history exists. Steps: Type short ordinary query like ai, type predicate advanced query, or disable unifiedSearch.acpHistory. Expected result: No ACP History rows are appended. Verification signal: Unit/source tests around root_acp_history_query_is_eligible, append_root_acp_history_section, and disabled options. Scenario name: File-section regression guard. Start state: Main launcher has primary row, Files section, file rows, and Search Files continuation row. Steps: Type a query that also matches ACP history. Expected result: AI Conversations inserts after the complete Files section/continuation, not between file rows. Verification signal: root_acp_history_rows_do_not_split_files_section_or_file_handoff and root_unified_acp_history_contract. Scenario name: Root row actions. Start state: ACP History root row focused in MainList. Steps: Open actions dialog. Expected result: Resume/copy metadata actions are visible; selected action executes against captured AcpHistoryEntry. Verification signal: actionsDialog.visibleActions, contextStableKey=acp-history/{session_id}, and scripts/agentic/root-source-actions-matrix.ts expected actions. root-acp-history-feature-map Visual States State: Ordinary root search with AI Conversations hits. What is visible: Main launcher list; primary/root-file rows first; section header AI Conversations; rows titled from entry.title_display() with subtitle {preview_display()} · {message_count} message(s). Focus owner: Main launcher filter/list selection. Footer/actions/chrome: Standard main-list chrome; selected row default action text Resume Conversation; type/source metadata reports AI Conversation / AI Conversations. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: mainWindowPreflight.visibleResults[*].role=rootPassive, typeLabel, sourceName, stableKey, actionKind. State: ai: / conversations: source-filtered browse/search. What is visible: AI Conversations rows and source-filter status/chip rows; disallowed sources suppressed. Focus owner: Main launcher filter/list selection. Footer/actions/chrome: Source-filter no-results copy if empty; standard row actions if a row is selected. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: sourceFilters=["conversations"], filterIndicators, cached_source_statuses_snapshot. State: Focused ACP History root row. What is visible: Selected row highlight on conversation title; preview/message-count subtitle; action affordance reads Resume Conversation. Focus owner: Main list selected row while input remains launcher-owned. Footer/actions/chrome: Main-list footer/action hint; Cmd+K/shared action dialog available. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: selectedResultKey=acp-history/{session_id}, selectedResultRole=rootPassive. State: Root actions dialog for ACP History. What is visible: Actions for resume/copy title/copy session id/copy preview. Focus owner: Actions dialog. Footer/actions/chrome: Popup chrome; close restores MainList focus. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: actionsDialog.visibleActions, contextStableKey=acp-history/{session_id}. State: Resumed Agent Chat. What is visible: Agent Chat surface with saved conversation loaded, or fallback seeded from first message if shared resume cannot load the saved transcript. Focus owner: ACP Chat view/composer. Footer/actions/chrome: ACP-owned footer/actions, not root launcher footer. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: ACP state receipt / getAcpState session or message evidence. State: Adjacent ACP History browser empty/list. What is visible: acp-history-list, or No conversation history / No conversations match your filter. Focus owner: ACP History built-in view. Footer/actions/chrome: Built-in ACP History footer. Accessibility/automation target if applicable: ACP_HISTORY_POPUP_AUTOMATION_ID / built-in view receipts where available; not owned by root rows. Invariants And Regression Risks Invariant: ACP History root rows are passive launcher results, never primary/promoted results. Why it matters: Saved conversations must not steal intent from commands, scripts, apps, skills, windows, actions, or file rows. Files/tests that pin it: lat.md/builtins#Root Unified Search ACP History; src/scripts/search/unified.rs; src/scripts/grouping.rs; tests/source_audits/root_unified_acp_history_contract.rs. Invariant: ACP rows insert after primary/root file rows and before fallback handoff rows. Why it matters: Preserves root launcher intent and fallback discoverability. Files/tests that pin it: append_root_acp_history_section; append_root_passive_section; root_acp_history_rows_insert_after_primary_rows_before_fallbacks. Invariant: ACP rows must not split the Files section or Search Files continuation row. Why it matters: Prevents the exact passive-source regression called out as critical in verification guidance. Files/tests that pin it: root_acp_history_rows_do_not_split_files_section_or_file_handoff; root_unified_acp_history_uses_passive_grouping_contract; verification guidance. root-acp-history-feature-map Invariant: ACP History rows are stable but non-bindable. Why it matters: Selection restoration/action context need stable identity, but saved conversations should not become shortcut aliases/launcher commands. Files/tests that pin it: AcpHistoryMatch; SearchResult::AcpHistory; history_result_key/stable_selection_key as acp-history/{session_id}; launcher_command_id => None; root_unified_acp_history_result_is_stable_and_non_bindable. Invariant: Enter path uses only the shared ACP history resume helper. Why it matters: Root search must not fork ACP resume semantics from the built-in history browser. Files/tests that pin it: src/app_impl/selection_fallback.rs; src/render_builtins/acp_history.rs#ScriptListApp#resume_acp_conversation_from_history; root_unified_acp_history_enter_resumes_existing_helper. Invariant: Ordinary passive root search is cache-only and frame-frozen. Why it matters: Prevents blocking JSONL reads, late-result UI churn, selection movement, and frame instability while typing. Files/tests that pin it: search_history_cached; root_passive_frame_for_current_query; root_unified_passive_snapshot_contract; root-passive-frame-stability.ts. Invariant: Explicit Conversations source filters can browse even with empty stripped text. Why it matters: Source-only ai: is a user-facing browse path, while ordinary empty root remains clean. Files/tests that pin it: menu_syntax_source_filters.rs; source_filters.includes(Conversations) raises min_query_chars=0; lat builtins section. Invariant: Config/schema/default/audit parity includes ACP History. Why it matters: config.ts must expose only implemented source controls and Rust/TS must not drift. Files/tests that pin it: UnifiedSearchAcpHistoryConfig; acp_history_section_options; root_unified_config_schema_parity_contract.rs. Invariant: Actions dialog captures ACP subject before generic script fallback. Why it matters: Root passive rows need typed root actions, not script action leakage. Files/tests that pin it: RootUnifiedActionSubject::AcpHistory; RootUnifiedResultAction::AcpHistoryResume; root_unified_source_actions_contract.rs; root-source-actions-matrix.ts. Verification Map Source/static checks: cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_acp_history_contract -- --nocapture Run with the root file source audit to protect the Files section / Search Files continuation row regression. cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_source_filters_contract -- --nocapture cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_config_schema_parity_contract -- --nocapture cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_passive_snapshot_contract -- --nocapture cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_search_stability_contract -- --nocapture cargo test --test source_audits root_unified_source_actions_contract -- --nocapture cargo test --test menu_syntax_source_filters -- --nocapture Required repo gates for behavior/doc/test changes: cargo check --lib, cargo fmt --check, git diff --check, lat check. Runtime/state-first proofs: Use mainWindowPreflight after setting filter to an eligible normal query; assert visibleResults contains role=rootPassive, typeLabel=AI Conversation, sourceName=AI Conversations, stableKey=acp-history/{session_id}. Use setFilter("ai: conversation") / waitFor / getState; assert sourceFilters=["conversations"], expected visible rows/statuses, and no disallowed sources. Use rootPassiveFrame receipts and visible result fingerprints to prove cold cache/warm cache does not mutate the current frame. Use Enter on selected ACP History row and ACP state receipt to prove shared resume loads/focuses Agent Chat. Use actions dialog receipt to assert visible action IDs/labels and contextStableKey. Visual/native proofs only if needed: Screenshot only for row rendering/header order if state receipts cannot prove visual grouping. Native input only if a bug depends on OS-level keyboard/focus delivery; otherwise protocol setFilter, waitFor, getState, and getElements are enough. No screenshot is needed for cache stability, source-filter state, stable keys, or action IDs. Open Questions / Gaps Gap: Exact user-facing fallback when resume_acp_conversation_from_history cannot load the saved JSON is only partially inferable from the excerpt. Why it matters: Review agents need to know whether failure should show an error, seed first_message, or silently open ACP. Suggested next check: Runtime seed a dangling acp-history.jsonl entry and verify ACP state/visible copy after Enter. Gap: Source-filtered empty state wording for ai: is implied by generic source-filter empty handling, not pinned specifically for ACP History. Why it matters: Empty browse should feel intentional, not like missing ordinary launcher results. Suggested next check: State-first ai: with empty history plus one visual proof only if text/chrome is not exposed in receipts. Gap: Actions scope has mild tension: root search does not expose attach-summary actions, while root action matrix exposes resume/copy metadata. Why it matters: Future agents may accidentally add attach-to-AI/summary actions under the ACP History root row. Suggested next check: Add/keep explicit source audit asserting no root_acp_history_attach_summary / attach action exists. Gap: User-configured passiveSourceOrder behavior for ACP History is source-audit pinned generally, but not mapped as a dedicated ACP History user scenario. Why it matters: Reordering passive sources could accidentally violate the root file/fallback boundary. Suggested next check: Add a focused grouping test for custom order with ACP History still after Files and before fallback. Gap: Runtime resume proof is not named in the bundle the way source/filter/action matrix scripts are. Why it matters: Source audits prove wiring, but not the full user-visible resume result. Suggested next check: Add an agentic proof that seeds saved ACP history, selects ai: row, presses Enter, and asserts ACP session/messages state.
